National News Agency, London, 9th – The British Emperor today received Sir Miles Lampson, the British Minister to China, to hear a detailed account of the Shanghai war and the breakdown of negotiations.

Chaos on the Chao Chow Maru in Yokohama 96

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th – The Chao Chow Maru, owned by the Kobe-based Kanetani Shipping Company, experienced a sudden explosion of volatile oil stored in the ship's bottom while preparing to depart for Taiwan at the Tsurumi Pier in Yokohama this morning. The vicinity turned into a sea of fire, injuring six crew members.

Spanish Merchant Ship "Tie De" Wrecked 97

Reuters, West Africa, Lago, 8th – The Spanish merchant ship "Tie De" was wrecked off the coast of the island of Fernando Po in the Gulf of Guinea. Eight hundred passengers were forced to escape in lifeboats, but they are in a perilous situation because the wreck occurred in the most turbulent part of the Atlantic Ocean, which is also the most dangerous area off the West African coast. Two British ships have received the alert and are now rushing to the rescue.

Important News

Gu Weijun Speaks

Impressions of the Journey East 98

Compatriots in the Northeast are in an extremely painful position

Anti-Japanese forces will inevitably be eliminated due to lack of support

Hoping that both the government and the public will quickly awaken and unite together

Ping News – The League of Nations Investigation Team returned to Ping yesterday. Mr. Gu Weijun, the representative of our country, spoke freely with news reporters from Ping City at the Foreign Affairs Building at 11:00 AM on the 6th regarding his recent trip to the East. The record is as follows: "The suffering of the people of the three northeastern provinces is beyond the imagination of the people within the pass. This suffering is entirely under oppression. The people of the eastern provinces love their country no less than the people within the pass.

The Investigation Team travels by foreign car for a tour of the Beidaihe beach 99

Even under these circumstances, their suffering can be seen everywhere. One day after returning to Fan from Harbin, there was a student sports meeting in front of the Yamato Hotel. There were thousands of students parading with Japanese and Manchurian flags. A large part of them were Japanese students, and the rest were Chinese students. When the flag-awarding ceremony was held, they sang the Manchurian national anthem and shouted 'Banzai!' However, all those singing were Japanese students, and their cheers were thunderous, while the Chinese students all hung their heads in despair. The delegation felt very distressed by this situation. One day, I was strolling in the park, and there were many students strolling in the park at the same time. They lingered for a long time, wanting to talk to me and tell me about the situation near Harbin. At this time, there were already three people following me. The three people behind me didn't look happy after the students said a few words. At that time, I stopped those students from continuing to speak and asked them to write it down and send it to me. They were very sad because the opportunity was rare or they didn't understand what I meant. Everyone can see that the 30 million people are now in a very painful and unfree position. It is really because the civil groups are not developed and free, and cannot develop a sound organization. Once something happens, they are completely disorganized and cannot have considerable effective ability. As for the main reason, we must say that the country usually does not pay attention to developing the spirit of the people and the methods of cooperation between the people. There are some who are really resisting there, and several soldiers are well-known to everyone, such as Ma Ding, Li, and Gong. They are fighting, with strong enemies in front and no assistance behind. The transportation is not in their own hands, and they cannot contact each other. However, their efforts to resist are giving the local people a chance to vent their anger. This kind of resistance is a resistance for tongue service, and the opponent is an army with a very complete organization, very complete equipment, and extremely powerful equipment. Every time there is a conflict, the enemy dies one and we always die ten. They are still resisting, and every day they are fighting to preserve the eastern province. A few dozen, dozens, or even hundreds die every day. We are very sad that we cannot help them with their sacrifices. The day before yesterday, I said that if this continues, China will inevitably be subjugated, and this is not alarmist talk.

The investigation team tours the Western Hills and takes pictures 100

In fact, this is indeed possible, so we must find a way to save ourselves. They are using force to control the vast land and numerous people of the eastern provinces, and dealing with the low

The investigation team visits Lotus Mountain for photography 101

The Chinese army that is resisting them has no support, while the other side has a whole organization and uses the power of the whole country as support. The Chinese army will be wiped out by them, but it is only a matter of time. Now they are like birds in a cage, doing whatever they want to ordinary people without guns. The media is completely controlled by them, and freedom of action is also restricted. In schools, all schools above the secondary level are occupied by the army. Although primary schools have classes, their textbooks have been revised by them. They have deleted everything that they don't want primary school students to know. This method is a thorough method of encroachment and a method of cutting grass and roots. After ten or five years, the relationship between the youth of the eastern provinces and China may be completely unclear. The so-called government agencies have presidents, ministers, and directors in name, and even though they are run by Chinese people, only one or two Japanese advisors can have full power. The matters to be handled must be approved by the advisor. They command as they please, but everything is done by the Chinese to show the world that it is an expression of public opinion. On the other hand, in terms of military affairs, they are clearing the forces of resistance and increasing divisions of the Japanese army. If the Japanese army is not enough, they are recruited from the local area. At the same time, they are actively carrying out political organizations, such as reorganizing financial matters, using the finances of the eastern provinces to support the troops who cause chaos in the eastern provinces. If this continues, the eastern provinces will soon not only completely break away from China, but will also become a source of aggression within the pass. The loss of the three northeastern provinces is said to be a national crisis, but it is only the beginning of the national crisis. If the eastern provinces are completely lost, the same danger can occur in the northwest and southwest. Everyone must know the danger of the position they are in, and no one should boast empty words anymore. They must do it in a practical way. In the 20th century, the survival of a country depends entirely on real strength. China's vast land and large population are by no means a guarantee. We should redouble our efforts to build the country.

The investigation team takes pictures in front of the Zhang family building 102

If other countries use ten points of strength, we must use thirty or forty points of strength to achieve the same progress. What does the country look like now? Internationally, people think our country is scattered and chaotic. One side is fighting, and the other side is negotiating peace. The government is breaking off relations with Russia, and the local government is establishing consulates with Russia. Other unsound situations exist everywhere. I hope that the whole country, whether in or out of the government, will take the country as the prerequisite. If the country is prosperous and strong, the people can all be citizens of a strong country. If the country cannot do well on its own, it may even perish. At that time, both jade and stone will be burned together and everyone will die together. I hope the Chinese people wake up, understand the current danger, find a new way, unite the whole country, follow this road together, make the country strong, and preserve its due position in the world. Although the above is full of emotion, it is all what the conscience wants to say. There is no prejudice whatsoever. I always hope that everything will be based on the country as the premise, so that the territory can be preserved, and the 400 million compatriots will not have the pain of being subjugated."

Chiang Kai-shek

Coming to Hankou to supervise the suppression of bandits 103

Telegraphic order to the Pacification Headquarters: All recovered bandit areas must be treated with compassion and those who were coerced must be forgiven

He Chengjun issued a general order to the bandit suppression troops, urging them with three matters

Qian Zhuolun indicated that the General Headquarters will be set up in Bengbu

Hankou Correspondence: It has been rumored for a long time that Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, who also serves as the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, will come to Hankou to supervise the army. After receiving the news, He Chengjun, head of the Pacification Headquarters, immediately borrowed the Bankers Association as his headquarters and began preparations. He also ordered Ye Peng, the commander of the garrison, to maintain strict vigilance. The roads near the headquarters were also being repaired, and tattered slogans on the walls were torn down and washed clean. Other welcome ceremonies were all simplified. On the 4th of this month, Yu Feipeng, Huang Zhenxing, Lu Zuolin, Lin Xiang and others arrived in Hankou on the Jiangjing end. On the 5th, Qian Zhuolun, the chief of staff, and Chen Xizeng, the chief of general affairs, also led personnel from the general headquarters on the Jiangtian Wheel. However, Commander-in-Chief Chiang had not yet left for the festival in Beijing. On the 7th, a telegram was received from Nanjing stating that Chiang had already left on the Yingrui warship westward at 5:00 PM on the same day with his wife, Ms. Song Meiling, and guard Wang Shihe. The Yongshui warship followed as escort. On the 8th, another telegram was received from Anhui stating that they had arrived in Anqing at 1:00 PM. Wu Zhongxin, the chairman of Anhui, boarded the ship to greet them. They soon set sail and are scheduled to make a slight stop when they arrive in Jiujiang. According to naval news, Minister He Yingqin went from Nanchang to Xun and had consultations with Chiang. If he does not stay for long, he will arrive in Hankou before noon on the 9th. All the generals in Hankou are staying here to welcome him, and those in the defense areas will also come to Hankou to receive instructions. As for whether Chiang will be stationed in Hankou after arriving, or go to the front to supervise the army, or return to Nanking, it probably depends on the convening of a military conference and the bandit situation. However, according to Qian Zhuolun, the general headquarters plans to set up the central station of the Jinpu Road,

Page 10

Bengbu is the most suitable. Working in Hankou is temporary in nature, and the name is General Headquarters. He also said that Commander-in-Chief Chiang will come to Hankou to inspect and summon senior military officers, give face-to-face instructions, and then go to Henan via the Pinghan Road, and then to Anhui via the Longhai Road Jinpu Road. Whether this will be the case in the future remains to be proven by facts. As for bandit suppression in Hubei Province, it is currently going smoothly. Bandit areas are being recovered day by day. Post-war matters are being handled separately by the Pacification Headquarters, the Bandit Suppression Propaganda and Consolation Committee, the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs, the Qingxiang Association, and the Post-War Association. Commander-in-Chief Chiang also telegraphed the Pacification Headquarters to take good care of the comforting, and those who were coerced to become bandits should be exempted from implication. The original telegram stated: "Since the Red bandits have been causing trouble, the rural system has been completely destroyed, the people's property has been completely filled with bandits, the good people are afraid of fleeing, vagrants are either threatened or driven, the villages are deserted, and the fields are desolate. The suffering is really sad. In the future, all recovered areas should be treated with compassion and consolation. All those who were coerced should be exempted from implication," etc. After receiving the telegram, He Chengjun issued a general order to the various armies on the 8th to comply with it. At the same time, he ordered the various armies to pay attention to three matters during the tense period of bandit suppression. The original order stated: "In order to follow the orders, the way of governing the army is to focus on training. The spirit of training is to be constant. In the past, the Prime Minister was in Guangxi, and he gave lectures to the armies of Yunnan, Guangdong, and Jiangxi on military spirit education. In addition to elaborating on the three things of wisdom, benevolence, and courage, he repeatedly emphasized the two words 'determination'. Determination means being able to be constant. For soldiers, training is like daily diet for life. They cannot be separated from them in times of urgency. Diligent training can turn weak soldiers into strong soldiers. Neglecting training can turn restraint into a mob. Therefore, soldiers cannot be unprepared for a day, and they cannot be unprepared for a day. The various troops stationed in Hubei have been suppressing bandits for many years and have been fighting hard. They are still able to plan and consider both training and implementation at any time. However, there are also those who only consider one thing and lose the other, and abandon it as if it were lost. During this tense period of work, I have specially stipulated three items below regarding the urgent need to rectify and easy to implement, for your reference and follow-up. (1) Rectify military discipline. It is known that military discipline is the lifeblood of the army. This is something that all soldiers know, and they should always keep it in mind and not neglect it for a moment. Recently, the national treasury has been empty, the source of military pay has not been continuous, and the roads have been blocked and transportation has been difficult. Therefore, the various armies inevitably have the practice of collecting materials directly from the local area. It must be known that our people have already suffered the tragic disaster of the Red bandits, and they have also been subjected to the demands of the army. The burden is too heavy, and they are unable to supply. Therefore, there are complaints such as 'the bandits pass like a comb, and the soldiers pass like a wash'. The military and the people hate each other, and the accumulation cannot be calmed down. For the Red bandits, there are forgiving words. Once the people's hearts are gone, it will be difficult to appease them. They should be treated with compassion by the senior officers of each army, division, and brigade, and they should take care to rest and reassure the people. All matters such as preparing supplies, occupying civilian houses, and forcibly pulling civilian husbands are not the proper behavior of the army. If there are other methods that can be replaced, they must be avoided as much as possible. It must not be done in a willful manner, taking and demanding as desired, causing public resentment. In addition, arrogance and complacency are also to be suspended as strict prohibitions to maintain the military's reputation and maintain the relationship between the military and the people. (2) Pay attention to practical education. It is known that the Red bandits' whereabouts are unpredictable, and their gatherings and dispersals are impermanent. Moreover, they use traitors to transmit messages, which is extremely sensitive. Therefore, if you want to control the opportunity, you must quickly deploy troops. Traveling a hundred miles a day is more likely to win than traveling fifty miles a day. In the future, if our bandit suppression troops can get a little free time, they should immediately focus on training. For running, climbing mountains, and other actions such as marching urgently and marching strongly, they must practice diligently at all times and in all places, so as to develop a strong marching force, so that they can quickly rush to the scene once they encounter a bandit police, and not lose the opportunity. As for shooting methods and shooting discipline, they must be diligently taught and practiced effectively, so that every bullet will be fired without fail and orders will be carried out thoroughly, which is the most important. (3) Help the people to defend themselves. The army and the people should be integrated into one. If we get one people, the bandits will lose one people. If we lose one people, the bandits will get one people. It has been found that every time the bandit suppression results are achieved, if the military and the people can cooperate, the results will be more effective, otherwise it will be doomed to failure. Now, the counties and towns have established militias and organized self-defense, which are originally to supplement the deficiencies of the army, and should be supported for assistance. However, there are occasionally military personnel who do not understand the overall situation and specialize in recruiting militias or raising militia guns as their ability. This kind of action is tantamount to chasing sparrows for a bush, driving fish for a pond, cutting off one's own wings, increasing the strength of the bandits, and committing suicide, which is extremely dangerous. In the future, it must be strictly prohibited, and in the recovered areas, we must do our best to help the people and step up the handling of the regiment defense, so that the farmers and shepherds are all strong soldiers, and the hoes and thorns are all weapons. If this can be done, then on the one hand, the bandits can be restrained from looting, and on the other hand, they can be prevented from transferring and escaping. And on the side of the army, on the one hand, they can remotely support them, and on the other hand, they can avoid worries. It is a great convenience to get several benefits at once. Hu Runzhi's so-called using the people to defend the people, so that the bandits have nowhere to enter, is what he meant. The above three items are all important current plans. In addition to distributing the order, you must urge your subordinates to implement it carefully, and do not treat it as a mere formality. This is the most important. This order." (June 8)

Jiangxi, Hunan, Fujian

Bandit Forces on the Border of the Three Provinces 104

Zhu De's main force gathers in Changting and on the border of Jiangxi and Fujian

Mao Zedong leads peasant bandits to occupy southeastern Jiangxi

Peng Dehuai attempts to bypass the Hunan border and return to Jinggang

Kong Hechong still haunts eastern Hunan and western Jiangxi

Fang Zhimin's group is active again in northeastern Jiangxi

Nanchang Correspondence: There are currently five pseudo-military corps of Red bandits in the five southeastern provinces, namely, one Zhu De, two He Long, three Peng Dehuai, four Li Mingrui, and five Ji Zhentong. Among these bandits, Zhu De's strength is the strongest. The pseudo-Fourth Army of Lin Biao, the Twelfth Army of Luo Binghui, and the Eighth Army of Xiang Ying are all under his command. The next is He Long. All the bandits on the border of Hubei, Sichuan, Hubei, Anhui, and Hubei and Henan are under his command. The next is Peng Dehuai. All of the Kong Hechong's pseudo-Sixteenth Army in eastern Hunan and on the border of Hunan and Jiangxi are under his control. Li and Ji's forces are the weakest. According to front-line news, Li was assassinated, and his troops were taken over by Peng. Ji was in western Fujian and was designated by Zhu De as the AB regiment, arrested and killed, and disarmed and reorganized, but this has not yet been confirmed. After Zhu De withdrew from Zhangzhou, his main force concentrated in western Fujian and the area of ​​Changting Ancient City on the border of Jiangxi and Fujian. Zhu himself led pseudo-military agencies such as the Pseudo-Military First Army Group to be stationed in Ting for command. It is heard that the stock is stationed in Ting, and its attempts to invade Guangdong and Jiangxi are unclear, but due to the oppression of the Fujian and Guangdong armies, it will inevitably flee back to southeastern Jiangxi Province. Guangchang, Shicheng, Ruijin, Huichang, Xunwu, Yudu, Xingguo, and Ningdu in southeastern Jiangxi Province have not been recovered since last year's Hu Zu Wang and Shangguan Yun and other troops failed one after another and were re-occupied. Important bandit nests such as Longgang, Donggu, Tengtian, Huangpi, Xiaobu, Shima, Nakamur, and Gaoxingxu have all been restored to the state of Red bandit occupation. After Zhu's bandits entered Fujian, Mao Zedong stayed behind in the above areas to preside over everything. Mao used local peasant bandits as the basic team, which was very weak and could not leave the original defense area. Therefore, he is vigorously carrying out redification in the local area, confiscating land, houses, and other tasks. Most of Peng's troops were natives of eastern Hunan. The pseudo-Fifty-seventh and Fifty-eighth Armies once attacked Rugui and then attacked Jilong. They were defeated by the Wang Dongyuan, Liu Shaoxian, and Li Ming troops. They are now attempting to bypass the borders of eastern Hunan and ​​Guangxi and flee back to the old bandit areas of Jinggang in Ninggang, Yongxin, Suichuan, Lianhua, Guidong, Lingxian, Chaling, and Youxian. In recent days, bandits in Lianhua and Yongxin have been very active, which is not without reason. The Kong Hechong's pseudo-Sixteenth Army in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan has three divisions, the pseudo-Seventh, Eighth, and Ninth, plus the Guards Division that Peng Dehuai allocated when he was in Hunan. There are a total of two to three thousand guns. After being severely suppressed by Guo Rudong, Xie Bin, and Tao Guangluo Lin in Tongshan, Tongcheng, and Yangxin in Hubei, they fled to Zhajin Macao area at the junction of Xiushui and Pingjiang, and planned to enter Hunan to join Peng's bandits. The Red bandits in eastern Jiangxi were the Fang Zhimin Shao Shisheng and other groups. Since 1927, they have taken Mopan Mountain at the junction of Yiyang and Hengfeng as their lair, causing trouble on the border of Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui. All the counties under Guangxin and Raozhou have been ravaged. Last year, Jiang Dingwen, Xu Tingyao and other troops destroyed their old nest. The number of guns left by the group was less than one thousand. However, at the end of last year, a certain division collapsed, losing many guns, and the bandit forces surged again. Later, when Jiang's division moved to Hangzhou and Ruan's division returned to Anhui, Fang Shao took the opportunity to lead his pseudo-Tenth Army Zhou Jianping and the Peasant Self-Defense Army to capture Hengfeng, surround Dexing, disturb Leping, invade Qianshan, and even invaded Yujiang. Later, they were repelled by Li's division and Dai's brigade, but the poisoning of Yiyang, Guixi, and Guangfeng has not yet been eliminated. It is now heard that He Yingqin has transferred a certain division of Zhou's troops from eastern Jiangxi to the northwest, a certain division of Jiang's troops from Zhejiang to Shangrao, and a certain division of Li's troops will take a pincer attack with Jiang and Zhou, changing defense to attack. At the same time, he ordered the police teams of more than a dozen counties in the old three prefectures of Fuzhou, Guangxin, and Raozhou to concentrate their forces and launch a large-scale encirclement and suppression. Therefore, the suppression of bandits in that area is progressing gradually and actively (June 6).

Shandong Province

Strict Bandit Suppression and Qingxiang 105

The remnants of the bandits in northern Shandong are gradually being suppressed

A misunderstanding occurred with Liu Guitang's troops

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuju, chairman of the provincial government, plans to either recruit or suppress the remnants of bandits in southern and northern Shandong in the near future, in order to completely resolve them and expedite the Qingxiang. The remnants of the bandits in northern Shandong have been searched and suppressed by Sun Tongxuan, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression, leading Zhang Shulin of the Fifty-eighth Brigade, Li Hanzhang of the Eighty-fifth Brigade, and various troops, together with Zhao Renquan of the Northern Shandong Militia. The remnants of the bandits in Pingyuan heard the news and fled far away. They are now jointly suppressing the remnants of Xia Zhun. Hand-to-hand inspection Brigade Commander Lei Taiping also received an order at 2:00 PM today (7th) to take a camp of special service soldiers and ride the Taishan steel armored vehicle to northern Shandong to assist in the suppression. Li Shuchun, the deputy commander of bandit suppression and director of the Department of Civil Affairs, has been visiting Pingyuan, Dezhou, Yucheng, Encheng, and other places to inspect, summoning district chiefs, township chiefs, and town chiefs, to inform them of the meaning of truly suppressing bandits and exposing bandit classes in order to permanently eliminate bandit tracks. As for the western Shandong region, the giant bandits Zhang Heilian, Wang Changyou, and Li Douyin have requested to surrender and have been approved. They have been ordered to gather in Nan Shahe and prepare a column of empty cars to be sent to Yucheng for verification and reorganization. However, the bandits are located at different distances, with two to three thousand people, and it takes time to gather. Therefore, as of today, they have not yet gathered at the designated location. Counselor You Ziming and Deputy Director Meng Guangshan, who are handling this matter, are also in the mountains, supervising their gathering and resolving to complete the gathering in the near future and transport them to Yucheng for verification and reorganization. Han Fuju hopes that the bandits can be suppressed, and yesterday he specially established strict assessment of bandit suppression for the county magistrates. If a gun case is found once, a demerit will be recorded, if it is found twice, a major demerit will be recorded, and if it is found three times, the county magistrate will be dismissed. The telegram is as follows: "All county magistrates are aware that the banditry in various counties has been rampant recently, and robberies and kidnappings have been frequently heard. This chairman is concerned about the people's difficulties and cannot sleep peacefully. For the sake of truly supervising and urging, a special assessment has been established. The county magistrates are responsible for the local affairs and cannot shirk their responsibilities. Each must supervise and cooperate with the chiefs of the public security bureaus and the deputy captains of the militia to truly investigate and if the city and countryside are robbed or kidnapped. If the county magistrate is still negligent in war and defense, the county magistrate in charge will be given a demerit once, a major demerit twice, and a dismissal if more than three times. If the case is solved within half a month, the punishment will be revoked. If they dare to conceal the case and fail to report it, they will be severely punished upon verification. In addition to ordering them to comply, they are hereby informed in advance, and they must all be respected."

Also, Sun Tongxuan and Li Shuchun recently received orders to lead troops to northern Shandong to suppress bandits and clear the countryside in order to pacify the local area. Unexpectedly, the Shandong Garrison Army Liu Guitang, Guo Wensheng, Yin Shixi and other troops stationed in Gaotang and Yaozhan, because they were originally recruited from bandits, had a misunderstanding and alarmed each other, suspecting that the authorities intended to resolve them. Therefore, on the 6th, they surrounded the Gaotang militia, disarmed them, and tricked the county magistrate Zhang Kebao into expelling him from the country. Sun Li immediately reported the situation to Han Fuju and prepared everything, while still comforting them in order to avoid the corruption of the local area. Xu Peichan, the director of Liu Guitang's office in Jinan, also fled because of this incident. The remaining personnel have been captured separately by the Jinan Garrison Command. However, according to Han Fuju, after Liu Guitang and other troops were recruited, their military pay and all other treatments were the same as those of the Third Route Army. Unexpectedly, Liu still forced Shangtang Sixian to borrow money. The original intention of bandit suppression in northern Shandong this time was to pacify the local area. Liu Guitang was guilty and had a misunderstanding and alarmed each other. Now the army is ready, but he still hopes that he will realize his mistake and submit, otherwise he will only have to suppress him severely (7th).

Chahar

Finance and Economy 106

Inspection of the Report from the Director of the Finance Department to the Ministry of Finance

Annual Deficit Exceeds 1.3 Million Yuan

Hoping for Sino-Russian Restoration of Relations to Alleviate the Situation

Wen Guang, the Director of the Finance Department of Chahar Province, recently submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance regarding the financial situation of the entire Chahar Province. The report stated that the annual deficit reached over 1.36 million yuan. The only way to alleviate the situation is to restore Sino-Russian relations, thereby reopening the Zhangjiakou-Kulun trade. The report also provided a detailed description of the terrain and the people's economy of Chahar Province. The report read, "I have received your Ministry's decree No. 113, instructing me to comply. The Ministry has the legal responsibility to supervise the local finances of all provinces and cities. It is necessary to have a thorough understanding of the revenue and expenditure surpluses and deficits, as well as methods of rectification, in order to have a comprehensive and accurate view. The Finance Department's revenue and expenditure situation, whether it is surplus or deficit, whether the existing tax sources can be improved, whether the various economic expenditures can be reduced, and how to increase revenue and reduce expenditure to achieve a balance, must be reported in detail within twenty days after the receipt of this document. This matter concerns the major plan of financial rectification and should be properly handled. I have already issued separate orders. I hereby order you to comply without delay, etc." After investigation, Chahar is located in the central part of Inner Mongolia, with deserts running across it. The south of the desert is the territory of the Eight Banners of the Chahar Department, as well as the four pastoral groups of Mian, Shangdu, Left Wing, and Right Wing. The north of the desert is the territory of the five leagues and ten banners of the Xilingol League. The land of the Mongolian people in each banner has always been managed by the princes of each banner. However, Dolon is a place for trade between the Han and Mongolians, and it is also a necessary route for travelers from Rehe Zhangjiakou to Kulun. When Kulun is open, business is very prosperous. Zhangjiakou and Dushikou are strategically located border passes for a long time, serving as thoroughfares for the entry and exit of Han and Mongolian people. Zhangjiakou is also a central hub for the trade of goods between the Han and Mongolians. Therefore, the Qing Dynasty established three offices to govern it, which were subordinate to the Koubei Road of Hebei Province. In the spring of the 18th year of the Republic of China, the ten counties of Koubei were劃劃歸 Chahar Province, and the five counties of Xinghe, Fengzhen, Jining, Taolin, and Liangcheng, which were previously under Chahar Province, were transferred to Suiyuan. The current jurisdiction of Chahar Province is the territory of one county and three offices formerly under Koubei Road. This is the actual situation of the administrative region. In addition, during the Qing Dynasty, the various parts of Inner Mongolia were divided into governors and generals to intimidate their princes without interfering in their internal affairs, originally to show appeasement. The Chahar Governor did not reside within the territory of Chahar, but in Zhangjiakou, Hebei. Also, because he did not interfere in their internal affairs, and the Mongolian people lived by nomadism, moving with the water and grass, there was no land tax income to provide for government expenses. Zhangjiakou is adjacent to Chahar, being an important road for Inner and Outer Mongolia to enter Beijing, and a market for Russian and Mongolian goods. Collecting taxes on goods is sufficient to meet the needs of political and military expenditures, and the situation in Chahar is also easy to understand. This is the original intention of the Chahar Governor residing in Zhangjiakou. Although the four pastoral areas were opened up for cultivation in the early years of the Republic of China, the land is located on a plateau, close to the desert, with dry air and little rainfall, which is not suitable for farming. The cultivated land has been abandoned, and the whole area is desolate. Therefore, after eighteen or nineteen years of cultivation, it is still desolate. Traveling in the area, one often does not see any signs of human habitation for dozens of miles. At present, Zhangbei County is the former Zhangjiakou Office, Guyuan is the former Dushikou Office, and Dolon is the former Dolon Nur Office. Zhangbei and Guyuan are close to the border wall. In addition to farming and animal husbandry, there are also transportation and other industries that can be used to make a living. Therefore, it is not a completely desolate area. Dolon relies entirely on commerce and transportation, and there is almost no agriculture to speak of. As for Baochang, Kangbao, and Shangdu, the three counties were changed from the management bureaus of the reclaimed land. Due to years of famine, farmers have fled, and the population has decreased year by year. At present, each of the three counties has more than a thousand households and more than ten thousand people. Although they are called counties, they are actually not as good as the larger villages and towns in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The cultivated land that has been taxed can collect 50% in a year of good harvest, and less than 10% in a year of famine. This is the situation of the land tax population in the six counties outside the pass. Although the land tax in the ten counties of Koubei is not much, the actual collection is more than 90%. Therefore, although the total tax amount of the province is more than 600,000 yuan, the actual collection is only more than 480,000 yuan over the years. Last year was a bumper harvest, and the income was only 589,300 yuan. Therefore, land tax is the main source of local tax, but Chahar Province is an exception. The main tax source of this province has always relied on the Likin tax on goods entering and leaving Kulun. In the past, during prosperous times, the goods going to and from Zhangjiakou and Kulun reached about 70 million yuan each year, totaling about 140 million yuan. If 3% is levied, the Likin tax could collect more than 4 million yuan. After the Likin tax was abolished, the sales tax levied exclusively on imported goods could also yield about 2 million yuan, combined with local taxes such as brokerage tax and land tax, about 2.7 million yuan. Adding the national tax of 1 million yuan, the revenue and expenditure could be offset. Since the winter of the 18th year, Sino-Russian relations have deteriorated, and Kulun has been blockaded. Goods sent there are not allowed to be sold, goods that have been processed are not allowed to be transported back, and money from sales is not allowed to leave the country. Merchants returning to Zhangjiakou are restricted to bring back travel expenses of 200 yuan per person. It is estimated that the losses suffered by our merchants in Kulun amounted to about 60 million yuan. Since then, the commerce of Zhangjiakou has been in a slump, and many merchants have gone bankrupt. Financial institutions have been implicated and closed down. The customs duties and local taxes of Zhangjiakou have also been sharply reduced. At present, the goods entering and leaving Zhangjiakou are only limited to Inner Mongolia. The central area of the Inner Mongolia desert does not have abundant water and grass, and livestock are not prosperous. The value of goods entering and leaving each year is about 100,000 yuan each. When Jin Fang was in charge of Chahar, he was already suffering from insufficient income, so in addition to the production tax, he also levied brokerage tax, increasing the tax rate to be equal to the production tax, and transferring it to the provincial treasury. In the past, the county and local funds were allocated by the tax bureau to the county finance bureaus according to the original amount, totaling 135,500 yuan per year. It is estimated that the total local tax revenue for the previous year was 2,900,690 yuan. After deducting the funds retained by the county and local governments, the actual revenue was 2,771,300 yuan, which, combined with the national tax, totaled 3,763,000 yuan. This is the general situation of national and local revenue in the 20th year. In terms of expenditure, the provincial expenditure, excluding the funds retained by the counties and local governments, was actually 2,242,500 yuan in the 20th year, and the national expenditure was 1,394,500 yuan, totaling 3,737,100 yuan, leaving a balance of 25,900 yuan. This year's provincial government expenditure, starting from February, has been reduced to 1,728,500 yuan for the whole year, a reduction of 613,800 yuan compared to last year. The national tax financial expenses have been consolidated and reduced, saving 133,380 yuan. The two combined savings total 747,250 yuan. This year's military expenditure is 300,000 yuan per month, an increase of 2.4 million yuan compared to last year. It is estimated that the provincial government expenses will be 1,728,650 yuan,

The allocation of military expenditure is 3.6 million yuan, the national tax administrative expenses are 60,550 yuan, and the expenses for the Zhangjiakou relay station are 6,660 yuan. It is estimated that the national expenditure totals 3,667,220 yuan, and the two combined total 5,395,870 yuan. Last year's national and local tax revenue totaled 3,763,060 yuan. The revenue for this year has not started for long. According to the tax revenue for March, it is not as good as the same month last year. The prosperity of tax revenue depends entirely on the stability of the situation and the abundance of the year's harvest, which is difficult to predict. I will use last year's revenue as the budget for this year's revenue. The amount of revenue and expenditure deficit has reached 1,632,810 yuan. This is the actual situation of the inability to balance revenue and expenditure. As for increasing revenue, it has reached the point of exhausting the pond to catch fish and taking advantage of every opportunity. In the old Koubei Road, which is the poorest area with 10 counties and 3 offices, with a population of only 1.9 million, the local tax revenue reaches 2,771,300 yuan, with an average burden of 1.5 yuan per person per year, compared to the famous rich provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, where the average burden per person per year is no more than 1 yuan. In the most barren and bitter area, the burden of the people is more than half that of the people in rich areas. It can be seen that the people's strength has been exhausted, and there is no source to be exploited. The only way is to restore Sino-Russian relations, so that the Zhangjiakou-Kulun trade can be restored, and the sales tax can be levied on imported goods to make up for the shortage of military expenditure. As for reducing expenditure, the provincial government expenditure was 186,870 yuan per month last spring. In the 7th year, it was difficult to make ends meet due to insufficient military expenditure. After the establishment of the Beiping Financial Consolidation Committee, a financial meeting was convened in January of this year. After discussion, it was decided to reduce the number of institutions, and those that remained would also reduce their expenses. It is estimated that the Chahar provincial expenditure would be reduced by 51,150 yuan per month, starting from February. The monthly government expenditure was reduced to 144,050 yuan, including education, construction, law, science, police, and Mongolian Banner expenses, about 78,490 yuan. The actual expenses for provincial government, county government, and finance are only 65,560 yuan. Therefore, there is no room for further reduction. I respectfully report the huge financial deficit in Chahar Province and submit the comparison table of revenue and expenditure in the 20th year, the statistics table of national and local tax revenue, the statistics table of national and local expenditure, and the budget table of national and local expenditure for this year for your inspection. As for how to increase revenue and reduce expenditure to balance the deficit of 1,632,810 yuan, I respectfully request your wise plan for guidance and implementation. I am extremely grateful."

Guangdong Province

The Waters of the Three Rivers in Guangdong Province Surge 107

The North River is Most Dangerous

The Roadbed of the Shao-Ping Road is in Danger of Being Breached

The Military Bridge in Shaoguan City is Washed Away

Guangzhou Communication: Since the beginning of summer, various parts of Guangdong Province have suffered from drought. It was not until the end of last month that it began to rain heavily. However, the days have been overcast and the rain has not stopped. As a result, the areas that have suffered from drought are now reporting floods. Due to the continuous torrential rains in recent days, the mountain torrents in various places have risen sharply. The North River and the East and West Rivers have experienced large floods. The discharge of water is not timely, resulting in accumulated floods that inundate the banks along the river. The most severely affected area is the North River. The mountain range in the upper reaches of the North River is winding. The mountain torrents pour down, and the land is almost navigable by boats. According to reports, the roadbed of the Shao-Ping Road has been breached in seven or eight places, with the water depth on the road surface reaching five or six feet, making transportation extremely difficult. When the floodwaters reached Shaoguan City, the streets were also flooded to a depth of one foot. The North River is the confluence of the Qujiang, Lechang, Shixing, and Renhua tributaries. The water level is seven feet higher than usual. The river is turbulent, like thousands of horses galloping. The military bridge outside the South Gate of Shaoguan City was suddenly washed away by the water a few days ago. The bridge planks floated with the waves. Fortunately, the bridge boat quickly cut the cables and set sail, retrieving the bridge planks. The next day, workers were dispatched to repair it, and transportation was restored. Currently, the North River Defense Army, recognizing the importance of transportation during this military period, has strictly ordered local people to prepare for flood control works to avoid temporary chaos. For precautionary measures, the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway Bureau has sent engineers to inspect the roadbed of the Yuehan Railway line along with the road workers. If any places are found to be flooded, they will be repaired immediately to prevent accidents. Special attention is paid to the confluence of the Xunjiang and Lianjiang rivers. Due to the torrential rains in Qingyuan and Yingde in recent days, the floodwaters have also risen sharply. The floodwaters have washed away the rice fields in the downstream areas of Chini and Baini. As for the East River, Haifeng and Lufeng previously suffered from drought. Unexpectedly, the water of the East River has rushed down from Laolong and Longchuan in recent days. The water level in the northeastern downstream areas has suddenly risen by more than five feet. Various places were caught off guard, resulting in considerable losses. It has been found that the Juhu Pavilion in Laolong and Liujie in Heyuan, the Mijie Street and various markets in Huiyang, the county seat of Boluo, and the Dongxi and Luyuan Streets in Shilong, Dongguan,

All became submerged. If the weather does not clear up, the floods in the east will continue to lengthen. As for the West River, although the water level has risen, it is not as dangerous as the North River. However, low-lying areas along the river, such as Zhaoqing, Fengchuan, Sanshui, and Shunde, have been flooded. Moreover, the river is turbulent, and the waters of Genzhu Shoal in Shunde are particularly dangerous. Navigation is very cautious, and many ships have changed their routes to prevent accidents. The counties along the river, in view of the floods of previous years, are now rushing to repair the embankments, and the construction work is very busy. (June 6)

Qingdao Hailstorm Disaster 108

Hail also fell in Jiaoxian, and the Harvest of Wheat and Barley is Hopeless

Qingdao Communication: The weather in this city has been cold and hot recently. At about 11:00 am on the 5th of this month, thick clouds suddenly rose and filled the sky. At first, there was a downpour of rain and thunder and lightning, followed by a strong wind and hail. The hailstones were as small as pigeon eggs, medium-sized ones were like walnuts, and the largest ones were like chicken eggs. In a dense state, one could only see hail

and not rain. The ground was instantly covered in white, with a thick layer of about an inch. It stopped after more than 30 minutes. The accumulated water on the road submerged the knees. The telephone lines inside and outside the city were also destroyed and could not be connected. Many of the electric light bulbs on both sides of the road were broken. It was truly a strange disaster. According to

The Qingdao Observatory's news, due to the Mongolian high-pressure air attacking from Liaodong to Shandong and the Sea of Japan, this extremely dramatic change occurred. According to people from Jiaoxian, hail also fell in the county and the Haixi area on the 5th at the same time. It was the time when the two wheat crops were about to ripen, and the seedlings were all over the fields. Suddenly, after this hailstorm, all the crops and wheat seedlings were in a mess. The harvest is hopeless. Therefore, the farmers there are all crying out in pain. (June 6)

Beiping, 9th: The Student Union of the Normal University decided to strike from the 10th to petition in the South after the university president problem remains unresolved. Chen Lijiang has no intention of serving as Inspector of the Ministry of Education 119

He is extremely interested in studying mass education

At the 39th meeting of the Executive Yuan of the National Government on the 7th of this month, Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Education proposed the appointment of Chen　Jiang as a senior inspector, which has been approved. Currently, Mr. Chen is a professor and academic director of the Jiangsu Provincial Education College. According to Mr. Chen, he has recently felt the importance of mass education and is extremely interested in research. Serving at the Suzhou Education College, he especially feels that various undertakings are full of vitality, and the shortcomings of new education can be remedied. He believes that everything has a future in China. He hates all administrative duties and has decided not to take the position of senior inspector of the Ministry of Education. When the letter of appointment is sent, he will immediately return it and resign. Chen is from Jiujiang, Jiangxi, with a master's degree from the University of Chicago in the United States. He has served as a professor at National Wuchang University and Zhongshan University, and a member of the Jiangxi Provincial Government and Director of the Education Department. He is amiable and rich in academic atmosphere.

Regulations of the Ministry of Education

Matters to be specially emphasized in moral education in primary and secondary schools in the future 120

The Ministry of Education has stipulated the matters that should be specially emphasized in the moral education of primary and secondary schools in the future and issued a notice to the education departments of various provinces and cities:

Recently, our country is facing internal and external troubles, like water getting deeper and deeper, like fire getting hotter and hotter. If we do not seek remedy quickly, the future of the nation will be unimaginable. Primary and secondary school education is related to the foundation of the country and the nation. In this extraordinary period, teachers should share the crisis and intensify their work. Special attention should be paid to the moral education of students, so as to clearly identify the goals, use methods, and supervise young people and children, inspire their spirit, and vow to prepare for shame and national salvation. It is absolutely impossible to be lax or abandon one's duties. The Ministry has formulated the "Matters to be specially emphasized in moral education of primary and secondary schools in the future" as the standard for training students. I hereby order you to forward it to your subordinates to comply with it and urge the departments to supervise it at any time to see the results. This order,

Matters Requiring Special Attention in Moral Education for Primary and Secondary Schools Going Forward 121

(I) Training Objectives

Should promote the inherent virtues of our nation: loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, harmony, peace, etc. Simultaneously, special attention should be paid to:

(I) Vigorously eradicating cowardice and complacency, cultivating a spirit of bravery and striving.

(II) Vigorously eradicating dependence and perfunctoriness, cultivating the ability to be independent and responsible.

(III) Vigorously eradicating rashness and blind obedience, cultivating careful and thorough thinking.

(IV) Vigorously eradicating romanticism and extravagance, cultivating habits of diligence and thrift.

(V) Vigorously eradicating hypocrisy and disunity, cultivating a spirit of sincerity and solidarity.

(VI) Vigorously eradicating selfishness and self-interest, cultivating concepts of patriotism and love for the community.

(II) Moral Education Responsibility 122

(I) All teachers and staff in primary and secondary schools must earnestly share the responsibility for moral education, breaking down the accumulated bad habits of separating teaching from moral education. Each should formulate a comprehensive plan based on the relevant aspects of moral education and teaching in their respective schools, in preparation for division of labor and cooperation.

(II) All teachers and staff must have a thorough understanding of the current national crisis and must constantly remind students of it through various suggestive methods.

(III) All teachers and staff must live a life of hardship and endurance, practicing personality cultivation through example.

(IV) In addition to paying attention to leadership in training, all teachers and staff should fully utilize teaching opportunities (such as in language, mathematics, history, geography, natural science, social studies, physical education, etc.) to enhance students' systematic understanding and motivation for national humiliation and national salvation.

(V) Primary and secondary schools must hold morning assemblies every morning for short periods of instruction. The principal, teachers, staff, and students must all attend.

(III) Environmental Equipment 123

(I) Comparative tables of the population of China and foreign countries, as well as their land, sea, and air forces; comparative tables of education levels; and other various comparative tables.

(II) Maps of national humiliation, chronological tables of national humiliation, statistical charts of losses suffered in the national crisis, detailed before-and-after maps of places where the national crisis occurred, books and illustrations recording Sino-Japanese negotiations, and other materials related to the national crisis.

(III) Illustrations of historical events of our nation's national movements; illustrations of historical events of national movements in various countries in the modern world; and acts of bravery of the national army and volunteer armies in resisting the enemy in this national crisis, and others.

The above three items, (I), (II), and (III), are necessary materials for inspiring and encouraging. How to collect, compile, and set them up should be connected with teaching.

(IV) Spacious and healthy fitness venues, military training equipment (junior high schools and primary schools should enrich the equipment for Boy Scout training), physics and chemistry instruments, and specimens.

(Those who can make them themselves must do so).

(IV) Implementation Methods 124

Regarding physical education: 1. Senior high schools should implement strict military training, focusing on outdoor practical exercises. Students who fail military training should not be allowed to graduate. Junior high schools should intensify Boy Scout training, and primary schools should focus on Boy Scout training and health exercises. 2. Emphasize various group sports, national martial arts, and indigenous recreational games and sports from various regions.

Regarding community education: Guide students to organize self-governing bodies, cultivate group life, and emphasize strict organization to vigorously restrict individual freedom. Particular attention should be paid to cultivating habits of obedience and mutual assistance. The freedom of the nation and the people must be sought, and individual freedom must be abandoned. Seeking individual freedom within a group is selfish and self-serving.

Regarding intellectual education: 1. Emphasize scientific research, experiments, competitions, and achievement exhibitions. 2. Debates, speeches, and expressions of opinions should focus on the facts of national humiliation and national salvation. 3. Various research societies should focus on the status of our country's production and various national defense equipment issues. 4. Collect and display separately the necessary domestic products for clothing, food, housing, and transportation. 5. Research methods for identifying domestic and inferior goods. 6. Reports and investigations of important current events.

Regarding moral education: 1. Practice a life of hardship and endurance, reducing internal school labor. All labor must be jointly undertaken by teachers and students. 2. Save on banquets, refreshments, and snack expenses. 3. Promote the use of domestic goods. 4. Strictly prohibit romantic, ostentatious extravagance. 5. Take an oath to avenge national humiliation and save the nation, and train students to identify the career they should pursue in the future to prepare for saving the country and the nation. 6. At important gatherings, observe a moment of silence to mourn the compatriots who died in the national crisis.

The above four items are intended for both primary and secondary schools. In addition to the common necessities that must be paid attention to, each primary school should adjust the proportion of materials based on children's abilities and interests, and the content should be adapted to the grade level, with varying depths and difficulties, to guide them according to the circumstances. Even the various games and activities of lower grades and kindergarten children should be appropriately supplemented with materials related to avenging national humiliation and saving the country to cultivate them. All levels of training must be based on this principle, implemented earnestly, and must be sustained and consistent from beginning to end. Reviving decline and establishing the foundation depends on this.

Local News

In This City, Private

Regulations for the Establishment of Special Schools Announced 126

In order to handle the establishment of private special schools in this city, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has expanded and revised the five articles of the regulations for establishing these schools, and has submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval and to the Ministry of Education for record. It has been announced in the newspaper and implemented starting today. The regulations for establishing private special schools are attached below.

Regulations for the Establishment of Private Special Schools in Shanghai 127

Article 1. Special schools established by private individuals or groups within this city's district should apply to the Municipal Bureau of Education for establishment, and then be forwarded to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 2. The types of special schools are as follows: (1) Schools for the Deaf and Mute, (2) Schools for the Blind, (3) Schools for Children with Intellectual Disabilities. The following regulations should be followed for each school on the right. The words "Private" should be prefixed to each school's name.

Article 3. Private special schools of various types should apply for establishment in accordance with the following provisions: (1) When starting, the founders should first organize a board of directors, and the board of directors should fill out forms for the following items and attach two copies of the board of directors' charter, submitting them to the Bureau for approval of the board of directors' establishment. 1. Name, 2. Purpose, 3. Location of the office, 4. Regulations on assets or funds or other income, 5. Names, native places, occupations, powers, and addresses of the directors, etc. (2) Once the board of directors' establishment is approved, the school may be opened. Three months later, the chairman of the board of directors should fill out forms for the following items and attach two copies of the school's charter, submitting them to the Bureau for approval of the school's establishment. 1. School name, 2. School address, site, and building conditions (attached floor plan), 3. Source of funds and amount of income and expenditure, 4. Organization, staffing, curriculum, and various rules, 5. School equipment and various facilities related to teaching, 6. List of teachers and staff, 7. Number of students and opening date. (3) Special schools opened before June 30, 1932 may carry out the procedures in items 1 and 2 simultaneously.

Article 4. If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time with the approval of the Municipal Government.

Article 5. These regulations shall be announced and implemented after being submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government for approval and the Ministry of Education for record.

World Olympic Games 131

Our Country Cables Congratulations to the Assembly Chairman

Electric Timing Device to be Tested

India's Field Hockey Strength is the Strongest

Italy's Athletes Number One Hundred

Our Country Cables Wishes for the Success of the Assembly The 10th World Olympic Games will be held in Los Angeles in early August, as reported in this newspaper. Participants include more than 50 countries. Although our country cannot send athletes, Shen Siliang, honorary secretary of the National Sports Association, has decided to travel to the United States as a representative to show that our country is striving to follow in the footsteps of the advanced. Yesterday, the Association sent a congratulatory telegram to the chairman of this year's Olympic Games, wishing the conference success.

The Invention of the Electric Timing Device Accurate timing is most difficult in races, especially short distances, because a fraction of a second can make a significant difference. The 100-meter and 200-meter races take only about 20 seconds, so even a small difference can matter. The United States, which has the most advanced electrical industry, has an electric timing device that can solve this problem. According to a report from the Christian Science Monitor in Boston, an electric timing device that has been under development for some time has now been successfully completed. According to the inventor of this device, tests in the laboratory can measure five thousandths of a second without error. Columbia and Syracuse Universities tested it at Baker Field in New York last month during a track and field competition and were very satisfied. Former President of the American Athletic Association, Mr. Kerbey, said that if the tests continue to be satisfactory, he may propose its use at this year's Games.

Italy's Athletes Number 100 The conference received an official letter from the Italian Sports Association on May 24, stating that Italy had selected 120 athletes to participate in the championships of track and field, swimming, rowing, field hockey, equestrianism, boxing, and other events. The delegation is scheduled to arrive in Los Angeles on July 16.

Indian Delegation To Visit the United States The Indian field hockey representatives, a total of sixteen individuals, recently cabled the conference to enter their names, stating that they had departed from Bombay for the United States. It is noted that the Indian field hockey team are the incumbent champions of the previous World Games' field hockey championship. Recall that the final deciding match of the previous session was between India and the Netherlands. On that day, over ten thousand people were at the venue in the audience. As a result of the match, India defeated the Netherlands with a score of 3 to 0. The team has now boarded the Haruna Maru from India arriving in Japan. They shall be having a competition in Tokyo for a week, before switching to the Kameda Maru for their journey to America.

Australian Athletes Depart for the United States The athletes from Australia embarked on the Maryborough ship on the fourth from Sydney for the United States. Many people saw them off.

Sharp Decline in the Silver Market, Stagnant Atmosphere 133

Market Overview: Due to the continuous poor performance of the silver market in recent days, the market has been sluggish. Although there was a brief recovery at one point, it ultimately fell back and even continued to decline.

It is irredeemable. Observing the situation before and after the festival, it seems clear. Based on the current trend, it seems unlikely that there will be a turnaround. A prolonged decline is not fortunate for finance and various businesses. The future of the silver market also shows a loosening trend, which is of little help and is regrettable.

Silver Market Prices: The "silver dollar" morning market price improved by 7.5 cents compared to before the festival (i.e., the 7th), reaching 6 yuan, 9 fen, 4 li, 7.5 hao. The afternoon market fell by 7.5 cents again, remaining the same as before the festival, at 6 yuan, 9 fen, 4 li. The "silver split" opened at 2 fen in both the morning and afternoon markets, slightly better than before the festival, but the silver market remained as loose and chaotic as ever.

Subsidiary Coin Market: The price of Jiangnan small coins has recently decreased in line with the decline on the market. Yesterday it fell by 2 li to 5 yuan, 9 fen, 7 li. Observing the Background of the Silver Decline 134

Prelude to the Abolition of Taels

The continuous decline in the price of silver this year has reached its lowest point to date. It seems to be the lowest, exceeding the minimum price of over twenty years ago (7 qian, 5 li, 1 hao and a half) by more than 1 fen. If there were no special background, this decline would not have been so severe. Although current funds are abundant, during the 31st year of Emperor Guangxu's reign (Qing Dynasty), the current silver reserves in June and July once exceeded 200 million (formerly the prosperity of Shanghai was not as great as it is today, it would have to be at a 4:1 ratio). In the prosperous conditions of Shanghai today, it would be not an exaggeration to say that there is 500 to 600 million, especially since there weren't as many bank notes. The inside story of the cause of the drop in silver is that there were rumours that someone wanted to propose the abolition of taels (and replace it with yuan, although this had been agreed to, it has not yet been implemented). Judging from the current situation, this proposal might definitely be tested. Otherwise, the silver decline would continue without limit, and the hidden consumption in society's daily life needs would be immeasurable. While not certain, we will wait for future verification.

However, the coldness of market demand and the non-negligible retail sales resulted in a decline of about 0.5 to 0.6 yuan compared to Tuesday. The future prospects may become even more sluggish.

Cotton Industry Conditions in Manchuria and Tianjin 143

According to a certain gentleman in the cotton industry who recently went to Manchuria, Shandong, Tianjin, and other places in the previous month to investigate the cotton industry, the situation is described as follows:

Manchuria: In the past month, colored fabrics imported from Japan through Andong have accumulated in large quantities, estimated at 10,000 bales, putting pressure on goods from Shanghai, resulting in no large-scale transactions. In addition, with the decline of American cotton and silver ingots, the sales route from Shanghai to Manchuria is becoming increasingly depressed. Also, Shanghai yarn in various locations along the South Manchuria Railway has a small amount of inventory.

Tianjin: The inventory of Shanghai yarn and cloth in that area is still small, and there is a considerable sales route. However, there has been too little rainfall recently, and the prospects for agricultural products are worrying. Traders are unwilling to extend credit, so sales have declined, especially for Shanghai-made products.

Qingdao: There is considerable demand in that area, but recently, Japanese factories in Shanghai are starting to operate, and it is feared that the market price will fall, so buyers are waiting and watching, while sellers are eager to sell. Market prices have depreciated, but there are still no customers. The situation in Qingdao is the same as in Manchuria and Tianjin, with many Japanese goods arriving, putting pressure on Shanghai goods. Sales are currently hopeless. The products sold by Japanese factories in Qingdao include cotton cloth until September and cotton yarn until June. The sales of cotton yarn are more sluggish than cotton cloth due to the import of Shanghai yarn.

Weixian: The sales of colored fabrics are still good, but there are no transactions of raw-colored fabrics, and sales are particularly sluggish.

Silk and Tea

Haining New Cocoons Shipped to Shanghai in Batches 145

Another 300+ Bales Shipped Yesterday

This year's early and late silkworms in Haining's various cities and townships have been damaged by the weather, resulting in a strangely poor cocoon yield. The quality of the cocoons is poor, and few cocoon traders have opened scales for weighing, and they are suppressing prices for purchase. Most silkworm farmers are self-baking and self-reeling. The fresh cocoons collected by the local silk cocoon traders have all been dried and shipped to Shanghai in batches. In addition to the 200+ bales that have already been shipped, Hui Tong Company shipped another 300+ bales from Changan Station to Shanghai yesterday. The total cocoons weighed and purchased by Shanghai silk merchants this year are estimated to be only 800-900 bales.

European and American Telegrams Show Silk Prices Still Low 146

Yesterday, there was still no turnaround in the Shanghai foreign firm silk market. European and American markets could not sell Chinese silk at factory prices. Telegrams showed silk prices were still low. The old silk in the hands of various manufacturers were heavily invested, requiring a loss of 500-600 taels per bale, and were all mortgaged to the financial sector. Overseas prices were not enough to redeem the principal and interest, resulting in a desperate situation. Silk sales have also been suspended.

Tea Market Downturn Unabated 147

Yesterday, in the Shanghai foreign firm tea market, Zhen Mei green tea from Tunxi, Suian, and Xi County, and Ying Zhuang Xie He Jin Tiao Tong Fu and other firms, all had stomach appetite for it. Needle Mei and Xiu Mei items were particularly active. The trading of red and green tea throughout the city was quite prosperous. However, in recent days, traders, seeing that Chinese merchants were eager to sell, became even more demanding with their prices. Yesterday, the market price of Zhen Mei, Needle Mei and other green teas, as well as Qi Fu red tea, fell by 4-5 taels to more than 10 taels. The trend of the tea market is not considered optimistic.

100,000 Foreign Rice Arrives, 4,000 Sacks of Wenzhou Coarse Rice

Zhenjiang Gang Continues to Handle Xiao Xiao Rice

Yesterday, the foreign rice market initially showed an upward trend as various guest gangs arrived in the market to inquire after the Dragon Boat Festival. Other firms had no movement apart from continuing to deal with each other within the street. The entire market only offered 4,000 bags of Xiao Jiao rice, priced at 10 yuan 5 jiao to 10 yuan 4 jiao 2 fen.

Guest indica rice is sold as soon as it arrives, and there is no surplus in the market. However, the market price has been affected by foreign rice, and has repeatedly weakened. A new batch of Wenzhou coarse rice arrived yesterday, with over 4,000 bags. The market only offered 400 bags, priced at 10 yuan 2 jiao to 10 yuan, which is also less than a corner compared to last week.

Marked Flour Market

Miserable Start, Excellent Ending 149

Yesterday in the flour market, after opening in the morning, the market for each month trended toward a miserable appearance. Foreign wheat quotations continued to shrink by around 3-4 jiao (Chicago's near-term fell another 5 jiao), and the sluggish environment depressed market sentiment, causing prices to fall by another around 2.5 fen. July, August, September, and October were all priced at 9 qian for customs entry, which shows the market's decline. When the afternoon market opened, July was at its lowest at 1 tael 8 qian 7.5 fen. But it suddenly rose, because although the major factories found themselves at a loss as to what to do about the slack sales, the continuous declines would make it harder for sales to improve, so the 6th month spot was priced at 1 tael 9 qian, and 7th month standards could no longer be sampled and bought. For this reason, market sentiment changed greatly, rising one step at a time, rebounding by 3-4 fen from the lowest morning price, a situation that seemed to be manufactured. In the end, compared to Tuesday's closing prices, the 7th month improved 5 li, the 8th month improved 9, the 9th month improved 1 fen and 2.5 li, the 10th month dropped 1.5 fen, and the 11th month rose 7 li.

Forward Wheat Slightly Rebounds Before Closing 150

Yesterday in the forward wheat market, after opening in the morning, the market for each month was as quiet as usual because the foreign wheat quotations continued to shrink by 3-4 jiao, so the opening prices of each month were slightly lower than on Tuesday by 3-4 fen. When the afternoon market opened, the market was still sluggish, until it was closing, when the rumored rebound in the forward flour market was very sharp, market sentiment shifted, and the prices for each month saw a slight rise. The 7th and 8th months were on par with Tuesday, while the off-season was still soft. Observing the future, before the various factories start handling new wheat, this stable scene will not be able to hold up. In the end, the 7th and 8th months were unchanged, the 9th month was slightly better by 1 fen, and the 10th and 11th months were slightly lower by 3 fen.
