Local News

Wang Jingwei Returned to Nanjing Yesterday 152

Important Meeting Held at Chen’s Residence Yesterday Morning

Cai [Finance Minister] Song and Jiao [Transportation Minister] Chen Have Not Yet Agreed to Resume Their Posts

Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei came to Shanghai to persuade Finance Minister Song Ziwen and Transportation Minister Chen Mingshu to withdraw their resignations. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, another important meeting was held at Chen Mingshu's residence. Participants included Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Transportation Minister Chen Mingshu, Railway Minister Gu Mengyu, Industry Minister Chen Gongbo, and Wang himself. They discussed the overall central financial plan and earnestly urged Song and Chen to resume their posts. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. It is said that Chen Mingshu's determination to resign remained firm, while Song Ziwen's attitude softened somewhat after Wang's strong persuasion. Wang felt that his trip had come to an end and thus took a special train from Zhenru back to Nanjing at 2:25 PM yesterday afternoon. Details are reported as follows:

The Situation at Yesterday Morning’s Meeting At 9:00 AM yesterday morning,

Wang Jingwei convened a meeting at Chen Mingshu's residence. Attendees included Transportation Minister Chen Mingshu, Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Railway Minister Gu Mengyu, and Industry Minister Chen Gongbo. Chen had arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning. During the meeting, Finance Minister Song Ziwen arrived first, followed by Wang Jingwei, Gu Mengyu, Chen Gongbo, and others. They then began discussing various issues. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. While the meeting was in progress, Vice Minister of Transportation Chen Fumu also arrived around 11:00 AM. However, he did not participate in the meeting and left after only two minutes.

Wang Jingwei's Remarks After the meeting concluded, Wang Jingwei and Song Ziwen were the first to leave. According to Wang's statement to a reporter from the Huadong News Agency, the resignations of Ministers Song and Chen were due to difficulties in their policies. When we retain Minister Song, we should also help him break this deadlock. As for Minister Chen, he also faces unavoidable difficulties in his environment, and we should also find ways to eliminate them. Today's meeting involved thorough discussions. Regarding financial matters, since military spending accounts for a large portion of the Ministry of Finance's expenditures, we intend to consult with all parties to devise a solution.

Round Table Conference and Resumption of Diplomatic Relations Wang then discussed the Round Table Conference and the resumption of diplomatic relations with Russia. He said that on the Round Table Conference, our side accepted the League of Nations' proposal to find a satisfactory resolution to the Northeast and Shanghai issues between China and Japan. Based on the League of Nations' resolution and our established position, we can participate in the conference at an appropriate time. However, Japan is now advocating separate resolutions for the Northeast and Shanghai incidents, which contradicts both the original scope of the League of Nations' proposal and the central government's established policy. The central government's original position remains unchanged. If Japan insists on separate resolutions for the Shanghai and Northeast incidents, our side will consistently refuse to participate. As for the resumption of diplomatic relations with Russia, the central government has discussed it repeatedly and has drafted concrete measures. Once the final decision is made, it can be implemented. We must recognize that resuming diplomatic relations with Russia and allying with Russia are two entirely different matters, and that resuming diplomatic relations and tolerating communists are also two entirely different matters. The central government is still carefully considering the matter, and it must also understand the current situation in Soviet Russia. Wang also said that the central government has always paid attention to the Northeast issue. If Japan continues to press, the central government will certainly resist. However, we should also prepare in advance. We only need to observe the current situation between Russia and Japan to understand the need for thorough preparation. Our resistance against external forces should be proactive, not passive.

Wang Returned to Nanjing This Afternoon After returning to his residence, Wang immediately telegraphed the two railway bureaus, ordering them to prepare a special train to Zhenru so that he could depart at any time. Upon receiving the order, the railway bureau dispatched a decorated train from the North Station at 12:37 PM, which stopped at Zhenru Station. Wang arrived at Zhenru to board the train at 1:50 PM. Those who saw him off included Wang's wife, Chen Bijun, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Railway Minister Gu Mengyu, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Guo Taiqi, Director of the Two Railway Bureaus Chen Xinghan, and Director of the Traffic Department Zheng Baozhao. Wang and others arrived at the station at 2:22 PM and shook hands with everyone who came to welcome and send them off. The special train departed at 2:25 PM.

The Attitudes of Song and Chen According to reliable sources, Finance Minister Song Ziwen claimed illness and resigned due to financial difficulties. Transportation Minister Chen Mingshu also submitted his resignation due to difficult circumstances. However, after Wang Jingwei came to Shanghai to persuade them to stay, Song's intention to resign had softened somewhat. However, Transportation Minister Chen Mingshu expressed his firm resignation due to various reasons. According to sources from the railway bureau, Chen will return to Nanjing today to handle private matters, which are unrelated to his official duties. Before a suitable candidate is appointed, the affairs of the Ministry of Transportation will be temporarily managed by Vice Minister Chen Fumu.

Wang Arrived in Nanjing Last Night Nanjing, 9th Dispatch: Wang's special train arrived at the station at 9:00 PM tonight. It is said that the trip to Shanghai was very successful. Hu Hanmin and Wu Chaochu are doing their best to mediate the Guangdong affairs, and it is hoped that there will be no military conflict. Also, it is said that Wang has agreed to discuss Sun Ke's proposal to reform party affairs at the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. Sun plans to come to Nanjing after the Third Plenary Session adopts his proposal. He will not take office as President of the Legislative Yuan in the near future.

Yesterday, West of the Shajing Port

Sudden Deployment of Japanese Troops 155

Merchants and People Panicked and Closed Their Businesses

Chinese Police on Alert Thankfully Nothing Happened

The Dagong News Agency reported that at around 5:30 PM yesterday, in the area west of Shajing Hong, under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District and Third Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, where police power had not yet been accepted, two trucks of Japanese troops suddenly arrived and

deployed posts along the embankment, from Xiangyan Bridge to Hujia Mu Bridge and Qimei Road, checking pedestrians, searching door to door, and erecting barbed wire at Hujia Mu Bridge, cutting off traffic. For a time, people were in a state of panic, and shops closed their doors one after another. The Fifth District and Third Precinct Chief Wu Tingxun supervised the police officers and the Shanghai-Beiping Security Team to be on strict alert. Fortunately, no disturbances occurred, and local order remained normal. The following is a transcript of the report from Wu Tingxun, Chief of the Fifth District and Third Precinct, to the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau Receiving Committee: "It is reported that at around 5:30 PM this afternoon, in the area west of Shajing Port under the jurisdiction of this precinct, two trucks of Japanese troops suddenly arrived. After getting out of the vehicles, they checked pedestrians along the embankment and deployed posts, blocking Xiangyan Bridge and Hujia Mu Bridge with barbed wire and wooden frames, cutting off traffic. Five Japanese soldiers were also stationed at Xiangyan Bridge, conducting very strict checks, not allowing pedestrians to pass through. The people watching at that place were like a wall, and shops closed their doors one after another, with extreme panic. The chief has supervised the police officers and security team to be on strict alert and dispersed the idlers. The local area is still peaceful. In addition to telegraphing a report and conducting investigations at any time, the details of the Japanese troops' actions are hereby reported for review."

Zhu Qinglan

A Light Account of the Northeast Volunteer Army 156

Recovering Lost Territory is the Common Will of the People

Currently Occupied with Relief Efforts and Have No Time to Attend to Other Matters

Shanghai Gentry and Merchants Raising Funds is Another Organization

The Rumor of Recruiting Volunteer Army in Shanghai is Groundless

On the 7th, the Shanghai newspapers reported that "Zhu Qinglan is the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Volunteer Army," and the Japanese newspapers reported that "The Northeast Volunteer Army is recruiting soldiers in Shanghai and will sneak into Manchukuo." Yesterday, the reporter specifically visited Zhu to inquire about the truth of the reports in the two newspapers. Zhu replied that the Northeast is our country's territory, and the Japanese warlords occupied it by force and then organized a puppet state, wanting to permanently occupy our Northeast by the means of exterminating Korea. The people of the whole country are deeply saddened and hope that the government will recover the lost territory as soon as possible, which is the common will of the people. However, I am focused on handling relief work. At this time when the harvest is not yet in and the old grain is gone, the disaster victims are extremely distressed, and I am currently trying to find ways to provide relief. I really have no time to attend to other matters. As for the Shanghai gentry and merchants raising funds to aid the Northeast Army, the report said that it is another organization. The talk of recruiting a volunteer army in Shanghai is even more groundless. The Northeast is full of patriotic people, so why recruit in the South again? Moreover, the climate and geography of the North are not familiar to the people of the South. The reports in the Japanese newspapers are purely fabricated and are just sensational tactics.

Nomura, Shiozawa, Uematsu, etc.

Will Return to Their Country by Ship Tomorrow 157

The Japanese Navy that invaded Shanghai has received orders from its Naval Ministry to withdraw back to Japan. Therefore, Nomura, Uematsu, Shiozawa, etc., have decided to return to their country tomorrow. The details of this situation are recorded as follows:

Nomura Left the Hospital Yesterday Rear Admiral Nomura, Commander of the Japanese Navy's Third Fleet, was injured in the bombing in the New Park. After being treated at the Naval Hospital, it has been 41 days. His artificial eye has been fitted, and the rest of his bullet wounds have healed. He was discharged from the hospital yesterday. Because he was ordered to return to his country, he specially visited the naval commanders of the United Kingdom, France, and the United States stationed in Shanghai today to thank them for their condolences during his illness.

Izumo Will Leave Shanghai Tomorrow The Izumo, Rear Admiral Nomura's flagship, is moored in front of the Japanese Consulate and is scheduled to depart for Japan on the 11th (tomorrow) at 11:00 AM. The cruiser Tokiwa is also scheduled to leave on the same day. The Tokiwa is stationed at the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. Nomura, Shiozawa, and Uematsu, etc., will all board the ship at that wharf. The Japanese residents of Shanghai will be there to send them off.

The 15th Fleet Will Also Withdraw The four torpedo boats of the 15th Squadron under the Third Team have also received orders to withdraw. It is reported that several ships of the squadron have sailed to the Yangtze River and are now ordered to return to Shanghai. Due to time constraints, they will depart from Shanghai on the 13th and go directly to Sasebo Naval Port. At the same time, more than 700 naval soldiers will be withdrawn by ship. After that, the Japanese ships stationed in Shanghai will be under the jurisdiction of the First Overseas Dispatch Team, and a separate command will be established for the Marine Corps.

The Citizens' Federation, in order to hold a memorial service for the soldiers who died in the Songhu Anti-Japanese War in the city on the 12th, specially notified all citizens in the city to fly flags at half-mast for one day and wear black armbands to express condolences. Wen Yingxing Secretly Requested

Closing the Iron Gates of the French Concession 159

Strictly Guarding Against the Memorial Service on the 12th

The Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Wen Yingxing, sent a secret letter to the Director of the French Concession Police, Fébvre, yesterday. The original text is as follows: "Secretly addressed, it is reported that the Shanghai People's Anti-Ceasefire Agreement Aid Northeast Volunteer Army Association stated in a notice published in the newspaper on the 4th of this month that the association originally scheduled to convene a memorial service for martyr Gu Zhenghong and the martyrs who died in the Anti-Japanese War on 'May 30th'. Because of insufficient preparation, a notice was issued to change it to the 5th. Now, people from all walks of life have sent letters requesting to participate. In order to expand the scope, it has been decided by the entire Executive Committee to reschedule it to 10:00 AM on the 12th of this month at the West Gate Public Sports Field to hold a memorial service for the martyrs who died in the Northeast Songhu Anti-Japanese War. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will gather in teams to attend the meeting. This notice is hereby issued. It is reported to the bureau that

because the association had not been approved and was in a period of martial law, it published a notice in the newspaper on its own initiative to hold a meeting on June 5th, and it was ordered to be banned and the authorities were requested to temporarily close the iron gates along the Republic Road. Now it has been found that the association has recently rescheduled the event, and in addition to ordering the subordinates to strictly investigate and prohibit it, it should also be communicated. It is hoped that you will investigate and request that the iron gates along the Republic Road be temporarily closed on the morning of the 12th of this month in order to prevent and maintain public security. To maintain public friendship, this is addressed to Fébvre, the Director of the French Concession Police. Director Wen Yingxing."

Telephone Workers in the Concession

Presented New Conditions Yesterday 160

After Representatives Negotiated with the Company

The Company Agreed to Respond This Morning

After the telephone company workers in the concession went on strike, the head office and the warehouses of various district branches were heavily guarded. The strike committee

presented new conditions to the company yesterday, but there was still no solution. The company is scheduled to respond at 10:00 AM this morning. The details of the situation are recorded as follows:

Heavily Guarded Yesterday, the workers at the head office on Jiangxi Road and the warehouses of various district branches continued their strike. The inspectors from various districts organized by the strike committee were fully dispatched to work, and the order was very good. The Public Concession Police were ordered to strengthen their strict precautions. The iron gate of the head office on Jiangxi Road was closed. The Sima Road Police Station specially sent a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to be stationed under arms to protect it. The branches and warehouses in various districts were all guarded by the police, and the precautions were strict. The automatic machines in various districts were still talking as usual. Mass Meeting Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the entire

workers gathered near Fujian Road to hold a mass meeting, attended by more than 1,000 people. Five temporary chairmen were elected to report on the progress of the strike and to resolve (1) to welcome representatives to negotiate with the capitalists for victory, (2) to support the Workers' Protection Committee, (3) to oppose any mediation and let the strike committee directly negotiate with the capitalists, and (4) to schedule a reception for reporters at the Xinghualou on Sima Road at 2:00 PM on the 10th to report on the origins of the strike.

New Conditions Presented The strike committee presented the following new conditions to the company yesterday: The workers have been serving your company, and their wages are meager, and their lives are miserable. This is well known to your company and people from all walks of life. When the Shanghai January 28th Incident occurred this year, Chinese and foreign residents in the war zone fled to safe areas, but the workers disregarded their lives and families and continued to work for your company in the midst of gunfire. However, your company did not reward the workers for this action, but canceled the old practice of increasing wages every April on Sundays. At the same time, the company fired a large number of workers. After the dismissal, not only was no severance pay given, but the savings that the workers had accumulated over the years were often deducted and confiscated by the company for various reasons, and it was planned to buy and hire White Russians to replace the work of the workers. This kind of oppression and exploitation has made the workers unable to bear it, and other oppressions and exploitations cannot be described in words. Therefore, the workers announced a general strike at 7:00 PM on June 7th and put forward the following conditions, requesting the company to fully agree to implement the six required conditions within 18 hours and to recognize the preliminary agreement between labor and capital, so as to resolve the issue as soon as possible. Otherwise, the strike will be prolonged and expanded, and your company shall be fully responsible. (1) Oppose the dismissal of workers, immediately restore the jobs of the workers who were dismissed after May 30th this year, and pay the wages of the workers who were dismissed during the period of dismissal. (2) Regardless of new or old workers, increase wages uniformly according to the following proportions: increase 10 yuan below 20 yuan, increase 8 yuan above 30 yuan, and increase 5 yuan below 40 yuan. (3) Wages shall be paid as usual during the strike. (4) Recognize the trade union as the full representative of the workers. The company shall subsidize the trade union with 600 yuan per month for expenses and provide a office. In the future, the trade union shall be responsible for handling any labor-capital relations. (5) Female telephone operators shall rest for two months before and after production, and wages shall be paid as usual, and a production fee of 50 yuan shall be paid. (6) Please issue the savings and severance pay for the workers who were dismissed after the January 28th Incident and before May 30th this year. It is hoped that the company can understand the actual situation of the workers, fully sign and answer, and immediately implement the following articles. It is hoped that the workers will sign and acknowledge the following articles as a preliminary agreement for future labor-capital changes. (1) According to the current working hours, no excuses shall be made to increase them again, and workers may again request a seven-hour working day for female workers and a six-hour working day for young female workers. (2) In addition to fulfilling the wage increase this time, (3) Holidays and various trade union holidays shall be taken as usual, and the cancellation of Sunday holidays shall be opposed. Wages shall be doubled for work during holidays. (4) The savings and six months' severance pay shall be kept by the workers themselves. (5) If a worker is injured or disabled on duty, a pension equivalent to one year's wages shall be paid until the injury is healed and work is resumed, or for life after the age of 50 without working, and a pension shall be provided. (6) If a worker dies on duty, a pension of 50 yuan shall be paid (7) During periods of illness and marriage leave, wages shall be paid as usual, and expenses for medical treatment shall be paid. They shall not be dismissed if they recover from illness. In addition to the existing external doctors for seeing patients, Chinese doctors shall be hired. (8) Raincoats shall be issued to outdoor workers on rainy days, and indoor and outdoor workers shall be subsidized with 4 yuan per month for transportation expenses, and double salaries shall be paid at the end of the year. (9) Workers in air-conditioned rooms shall have the same meal time as ordinary workers. (10) The working

time of workers in the stove room shall be the same as that of ordinary workers. (11) Work shall not be transferred casually, and workers in each room shall not be transferred to do odd jobs. (12) If the company hires new workers, the trade union shall first introduce unemployed telephone workers to supplement the workforce. (13) The employment of White Russians shall be opposed. (14) The company shall oppose increasing telephone charges for users. Shanghai Telephone Workers' Strike Committee and all more than 3,000 workers. June 9.

Negotiations Began The strike committee, according to the decision of the meeting, appointed four representatives, Pan Dingquan, Xu Shijie, Ye Gongxing, Zheng Luojie, etc., to go to the telephone company at the corner of Jiangxi Road and Hankou Road at 2:30 PM yesterday to present the terms of treatment, totaling 14 items. Because the manager was out,

Chief Engineer Watson received them. He first advised all the workers to return to work before negotiating the conditions. The workers demanded that the company accept the conditions before returning to work, so the two sides were at odds. Later, the engineer agreed to consult with the manager and scheduled a response at the New Central Bank on Fujian Road at 10:00 AM today. The representatives withdrew at 4:00 PM.

Response Today The telephone company workers at the head office and various district branches gathered at the New Central Bank on Fujian Road at 2:00 PM yesterday under the order of the strike committee. Upon hearing the news, the police immediately sent a large number of Chinese and Western armed detectives to maintain order. About 400 workers gathered and went to the head office because the representatives were at the head office on Jiangxi Road, standing on the side of the road, waiting quietly for news of the negotiations. When all the representatives withdrew, they declared to the workers that they would wait for the company's response on Fujian Road tomorrow (the 10th). So the workers went along Jiujiang Road, with Chinese and Western detectives behind them, maintaining order, fearing that the workers would gather again.

The Workers' Representatives Refuted Yesterday, the members of the strike committee issued a statement refuting the company's statement, saying: (1) The capitalists said that the workers did not give prior notice, but the workers had already proposed conditions for improving treatment in the name of all the workers last year, but the capitalists refused. Now, in view of the lack of security in life, they are carrying out a strike. (2) The capitalists said that the strike was to restore the work of dismissed workers, which is an attempt to divide the unity of the workers in the industry. (3) The capitalists said that the company has always paid special attention to the welfare of employees, which is a deceptive tactic. (4) The company said that the striking workers destroyed the machines, which is completely untrue. It is a rumor that the company is attacking the workers. If this is really the case, how can the automatic machines talk?

Notice from the Strike Committee The strike committee notified all members yesterday, saying: For the purpose of notification, the strike committee

resolved yesterday (the 8th) to send representatives to negotiate with the capitalists, but without results. Another discussion will be held at 10:00 AM tomorrow. If the capitalists still do not have a satisfactory response, then it is necessary to continue the strike. It is scheduled for 7:00 AM on the 10th (Friday), and all our striking workers shall gather in front of the gate on Fujian Road to welcome the representatives and prepare for a third negotiation with the capitalists.

Responding to the Strike After the Chang'an Road Chinese Electric Company in Zhabei, which contracted for the automatic machines of the concession telephone company, received a letter from the strike committee calling on all the workers of the company to provide assistance, about 40 workers from the company who worked at the Fujian Road Telephone Branch were dispatched at about 8:00 AM yesterday. It is reported that they have implemented assistance to the telephone workers, joined the strike, and put forward their own terms of treatment, which will be requested from the capitalists.

Company Statement The Shanghai Telephone Company issued a statement yesterday saying that although some striking workers attempted to destroy the telephone near noon today, they were quickly repaired and were still able to talk as usual. In addition, striking workers have repeatedly threatened the employees who went to work, and all of them have been reported to the police station. About 1,000 Chinese employees went to work today, accounting for more than half of the total number of Chinese employees in the company. The strikers are limited to the manufacturing, installation, and maintenance departments. This evening, Chinese workers sent two Chinese letters to the company, but the person claimed to be only responsible for delivering the letters and had no right to discuss the contents. The letters have now been entrusted to someone for translation.

Promoting the Glory of National Products

Expressing National Spirit

Wang Pingnan, legal advisor of the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products, and Chen Binghui, the 12th executive committee member, fervently patriotic and driven by righteous indignation, served as the commander of the Shanghai Citizens' Volunteer Army. Liu Manqing Set Sail for Hong Kong by Boat Last Night 164

A Farewell Gathering by Border Groups

A Lecture at Shanghai University

Ms. Liu Manqing, a member of the National Government's Commission for Tibetan and Mongolian Affairs, was recently appointed by the National Government as a special investigator for Tibet and Mongolia. Last night, she boarded a French steamer and left the country this morning to go to Hong Kong, then to Annam, and from Yuxi, Yunnan, to Batang, and then to Tibet, to investigate the current situation in Tibet and Mongolia, and to convey the National Government's plans for developing culture and industry in Tibet and Mongolia. She is scheduled to return to Shanghai in two years. Tibet and Mongolia are located in remote border areas, and are very isolated from the mainland. Therefore, Ms. Liu's trip is actually responsible for the important task of connecting national feelings.

Farewell: At noon yesterday, Huang Jingwan of the China Borderland Society, Guo Weiping of the Northwest Society, Hu Shuhua of the Northwest Problem Research Association, Liu Liangmo of the Borderland Research Association, Yan Ziduan of the Northwest Reclamation and Colonization Society, and Wang Weidan of the South China Plantation Company, etc., held a banquet at Gongdelin to bid farewell to Ms. Liu. Halfway through the banquet, Huang Jingwan stood up and said, "I sincerely wish Ms. Liu a safe journey, and I also believe that Tibet and Mongolia are China's natural resources, which urgently need to be developed. Developing industry and commerce is enough to save China, which is on the verge of danger. Ms. Liu's trip is actually responsible for this important task, because the most important thing for China at present is that the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted to the point of extreme pain. According to the customs report, last year the value of goods imported into the country exceeded the value of goods exported by as much as 500 million yuan, of which agricultural products accounted for the largest proportion. China has always been established by agriculture, and it has vast land and abundant resources, and rich mineral products. Now it has to rely on foreign countries, which is very dangerous. If we do not find a way to remedy it, China will perish even without the imperialists using warships and cannons. The way to save it,

is to revitalize industry, develop mineral products, and after the development of industry and mineral products, all the materials needed will not have to be supplied by others, so our comrades of the People's Livelihood Improvement Society are determined to engage in this, and also hope that Ms. Liu will give good instructions in the future, and hope that comrades in this area and Tibet and Mongolia will often interact with each other to seek cooperation, and benefit the nation, which depends on Ms. Liu's efforts." Then Ms. Chen Yongsheng of Shanghai University delivered a speech, roughly saying that there are many young people in Shanghai who hope to go to Tibet and Mongolia to engage in development work, which will not only be enough to recover rights and interests, but also to relieve the unemployment phenomenon. Please Ms. Liu go to Tibet and Mongolia to publicize and arrange in advance, so that the young people here can go, and so on. Later, Ms. Liu gave a thank-you speech, roughly saying, "Today, I am very grateful and honored for the kindness of various border groups and the instructions of the gentlemen of the educational news circles. The task of my re-entering Tibet and Mongolia is to accept the central government's investigation of the recent situation in Tibet and Mongolia, and to convey the culture here to Tibet and Mongolia, because I am a Tibetan, and I am more able to understand the situation in Tibet and Mongolia. However, my knowledge is shallow, and I still need your guidance at any time. The next time I come east, I plan to bring several young people from Tibet and Mongolia to study here, in order to develop the people's wisdom in the border areas. When the transportation is slightly more convenient, I hope that you will also travel to Tibet and Mongolia to give more guidance." The banquet ended after 3 pm, and they took photos and dispersed.

Lecture: Shanghai University has always attached great importance to promoting going to the border areas, and has long had an organization called the Border Problem Research Society. The society heard yesterday that Ms. Liu Manqing, a special investigator sent by the central government to investigate Tibet and Mongolia, had arrived in Shanghai, and specially invited her to give a lecture at the school. First, Mr. Liu Liangmo delivered a speech to introduce her, followed by Ms. Liu's speech, roughly saying, "My trip to Tibet and Mongolia again is to complete the mission of the Republic of China in 1918, to promote the virtue of the central government, to strengthen their inward-looking heart, to consolidate our country, but the disputes in Tibet are still difficult to resolve, and in reality, there is still much isolation, and all the people in Tibet are under the oppression of the Sichuan-Tibet army,

especially in dire straits. In terms of Tibetan education, it is still very young, with no Chinese schools, but recently the Dalai Lama has often sent students to study in the UK, which is quite able to take the best of others and make up for our shortcomings, and his worship of Buddhism, with temples everywhere, is still the same as before. If its folk customs are honest and generous, and its treasures are abundant, and its territory is vast, it is indeed China's natural barrier. The government should find ways to appease it, and not allow it to withdraw from the vassal state, and young people should especially be encouraged to go to Tibet and Mongolia, to open up the intelligence of others and to seek the development of our own careers." The words were very sharp and moving, and the flavor was timeless. It is said that after the lecture, Ms. Liu discussed various issues in Tibet and Mongolia with the students of the school, and gave detailed explanations. By the time the meeting adjourned, the sun had already set.

Jardine Matheson & Co.

Willing to Yield the Lotus Pond 165

The Result of Negotiations with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

The British company Jardine Matheson & Co. established a lighter on the Lotus Pond Jiang surface in Zhenjiang, occupying our Jiang surface water rights. This incident occurred in 1915, and it has been more than ten years since then. The water surface rights there belong to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Over the years, negotiations have taken place, but the British company refused to return it. It was not until now that General Manager Li Weihou regained it. The details of this matter are as follows:

The Process of Being Occupied: The British company Jardine Matheson & Co. has the most ships sailing on the Yangtze River, and Zhenjiang is an important commercial port. Ships must dock up and down. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has built a wharf on the Jiang surface, and in front of it is the Lotus Pond, which is the most important area for ship docking. In 1915, the Zhenjiang Customs Superintendent circled the Jiang surface to Jardine Matheson, and the area occupied was huge. Jardine Matheson placed a lighter on the Jiang surface and constructed works. For more than ten years, the Jiang surface there was suddenly occupied by the British company.

Negotiation Situation: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has a large business in Zhenjiang. The Lotus Pond Jiang surface is located in front of the wharf and warehouse, and its water surface rights belong to the company. Since it was occupied by Jardine Matheson, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company negotiated with the British company in 1918 based on reasons, and tried to recover it. At that time, Jardine Matheson claimed that it was assigned by the Customs and not occupied by itself, and refused to return it. When Zhao Tieqiao took office as the Commissioner for Reorganizing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in 1930, the old case was brought up again. He sent Section Chief Wang Yunzhang and Shipping Section Chief Wang Pengmeng to negotiate with Jardine Matheson repeatedly, and argued with the Zhenjiang Customs Superintendent. At that time, Jardine Matheson proposed that it could be relocated, but it had to recognize all construction costs, which would cost about 200,000 yuan, and the matter was shelved.

Implementation of Recovery: This time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was reorganized, and Chairman of the Board Li Weihou was transferred to the position of General Manager. After taking office, he checked the handover volumes and found that the Lotus Pond Jiang surface was occupied by foreign companies, which not only affected the company's business, but also hindered national sovereignty. Therefore, General Manager Li still sent Wang Yunzhang to handle the recovery of the Jiang surface. On the one hand, he argued with Zhihe, and on the other hand, he put forward reasons, requesting the Zhenjiang Customs Superintendent to designate a new site for Jardine Matheson's lighter location. After a month, it was finally successful. Now Jardine Matheson has agreed to dismantle the lighter on the Lotus Pond water surface and return it to the company, but the affiliated piles and chains in the lighter's works are priced and bought back by the company, which costs very little. The case, which had been pending for more than ten years, has been resolved at once.

The Ninghai Warship Built in Japan Will Arrive in Shanghai Next Week 166

The Ministry of the Navy ordered the Ninghai cruiser from Japan in February of last year. It was launched in Japan on October 10 of last year. Half a year has passed since then, and most of the project has been completed. A few days ago, Deputy Minister of the Navy Li Shijia went to Japan to inspect it,

and returned to Shanghai yesterday. It is scheduled to go to Japan again next week to lead the ship to Shanghai to raise the flag and return to the team. The ship's displacement is 3,000 tons, its length is 330 feet, its width is 39 feet, its draft is 15 feet, its speed is 30 nautical miles per hour, its armament equipment includes main guns of 5.5 inches, three twin-mounted turrets, six 8-inch anti-aircraft guns, two sea searchlights, four torpedo launchers, ten machine guns, and one aircraft. It is said to be the crown of our ships.

The Problem of Fire Insurance Compensation in Zhabei 168

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Has Scheduled Mediation

Most of the houses in the Zhabei war zone were destroyed during the fierce fighting between the Chinese and Japanese sides. However, some of them were directly destroyed by artillery fire, but most of them were not directly related to the war. Therefore, the affected households have successively claimed compensation from Chinese and foreign insurance companies. However, the insurance industry stated that this was a war disaster and was not responsible for compensation. Therefore, the affected households organized the Shanghai Municipal Disaster Area Fire Insurance Compensation Promotion Association to negotiate with Chinese and foreign insurance companies on everything, and also sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to uphold justice. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has sent letters to the Chinese Insurance Industry Association, the He Ming Chamber of Commerce, and the American Chamber of Commerce, etc., requesting that they resolve this matter with a position of justice. The Chinese Industry Association has expressed that it can negotiate with each other. Therefore, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has scheduled a formal negotiation on Saturday. As for the foreign companies,

most of the maritime companies are acting as agents, so they must decide after the agent companies have made a decision, and then find a way. Therefore, there has been no considerable reply. Yesterday afternoon at 2 pm, the Fire Insurance Compensation Promotion Association specially hosted reporters from various newspapers at Yizhixiang Vegetarian Restaurant to report on the progress of this matter.

Reasons for Requesting Compensation: According to the association's lawyer Tang Youwei, the total amount of insurance underwritten by each insurance company is about 13 million taels and 75,000 yuan, with more than 4,200 policyholders. Foreign insurance companies account for nine-tenths, and Chinese insurance companies account for only one-tenth. Among the Chinese companies, the one with the largest amount of insurance underwritten is the Sincere Company. The company has an office in Zhabei. The Commercial Press is covered by the company. The company has a total of more than 1,050 policyholders, and the total amount of compensation is 9.9 million. The policyholders have very sufficient reasons for claiming compensation now: (1) When the war broke out, there was already a sign of danger in Shanghai,

but the insurance companies did not notify the policyholders in advance, stating

that they would not be responsible for ordinary fire insurance; (2) Although some of the houses in the disaster area were directly destroyed by artillery fire, most of the houses were not destroyed by artillery fire, and most of them were burned down. Some of them were burned after our army returned to the station; (3) This disaster is actually a special situation, and the insurance companies should also be responsible for this matter in terms of human relationships.

Now, the people in the Zhabei disaster area are eager for this compensation to wait for the restoration of their businesses.

Declaration of the Promotion Association: The losses of goods and the destruction of industry and commerce suffered by the affected households in the Shanghai-Songhu area are huge and painful, and it is difficult to restore them. The funds for reconstruction and living expenses are the fire insurance compensation for each household. However, the Chinese and Western insurance companies often shirk their responsibilities and delay compensation, so that the affected people's insurance premiums are wasted and the insurance money cannot be obtained. The property is gone and there is no way to appeal. The painful situation is indescribable. The direct victims are the policyholders, but the indirect victims, such as shop clerks and factory workers, are actually ten or hundreds of times more than the policyholders. All of them are becoming unemployed due to the lack of means to recover. The impact on social livelihood is huge and significant. If each insurance company can understand the current situation of the disaster victims in Shanghai and the environment they are in, and establish a foundation for future cooperation with the spirit of benefiting themselves and others, they should have a considerable solution as soon as possible. However, the relocation has been delayed for a long time, and there is still no way. It is not only against human relationships, but also violates precedents. The policyholders are unable to calm their anger and have no way out. They are forced to organize this association. More than 3,000 households gathered without prior agreement, with a total insured amount of more than 10 million. They will unite the strength of the masses to give a considerable response, unite as one, and fight to the end, and will not stop until they achieve their goal. In addition to submitting reports to the National Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government for filing and relief, we also hope that people from all walks of life will give their sympathy and assistance. This is the declaration, and we only ask for your public judgment.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Letter Requesting a Crackdown

Wartime New Houses Increase Rent at High Interest Rates 170

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a letter to the Municipal Government yesterday, saying, "For the purpose of submitting a letter of request, we received a letter from the Cigarette Exchange Association on the 3rd of this month, stating that according to a letter from Shen Qixiang, the owner of our member Tongmao Tobacco Shop at No. 398, Yongxing Road, Gonghe Xin Road, Zhabei, our shop has been open for 12 years, and the monthly rent is 42 yuan. The house has four rooms, calculated as three rooms, and each room is priced at 14 yuan. The rent has been paid on time every month, and although there is no deposit, it has never been in arrears. During the January 28th Incident this year, all businesses were closed, and countless houses in the war zone were burned down. Our shop was burned down by a fire in the neighboring shop on the evening of March 11th, becoming a wasteland. All the goods and property in the shop were lost, amounting to more than 10,000 yuan. At that time, our shop declared to the landlord that the new house would still be rented by our shop after it was completed, and the landlord agreed. Now that the house has been built, our shop went to rent it, but the landlord repeatedly shirked, and finally replied that the rent must be 160 yuan per month, and an additional deposit of 1,500 yuan must be paid. Our shop was extremely shocked to hear this. The rent has increased nearly four times, and a huge deposit must be paid, which is beyond reason. Considering that our shop has suffered huge losses due to the impact of the war, we are planning to resume business and take measures to make up for our losses. Now, the landlord does not add sympathy and does not care about the old relationship

, and wants to increase the rent arbitrarily and add a deposit of 1,500 yuan, which makes our shop unable to afford it and unable to resume business. The losses are unimaginable. How can our shop bear this? We ask your association to uphold justice and give us assistance, so that our shop can continue to rent, resume business, and be extremely grateful." The above-mentioned information has been reported to the association. It has been found that the landlord should add sympathy for the tenant who has lived there for 12 years, and now he does not care about the old friendship and increases the rent arbitrarily by as much as four times, and also adds a huge amount of deposit of 1,500 yuan, which makes the shop unable to afford it, which is beyond reason. Moreover, the shop has suffered huge

losses and urgently needs to restore its old business to maintain its livelihood. Approved the letter for the aforementioned reason, and especially report the situation and ask your association to understand the difficulties of the merchants and give them assistance quickly to promote public friendship, etc. It has been found that the losses suffered by the stores and residents in the Shanghai-Songhu war zone are extremely serious, and it is necessary to plan for the labor to settle down and cultivate vitality. The landlords are also expending a lot of effort to build new houses in various places where their houses have been burned down, and they must raise capital. However, as the association said, the rent is increased by as much as four times according to the original rent, and a huge amount of deposit that has never been charged before is added, which is inevitable to take advantage of the danger and invite profits, making it impossible for the shops that have survived the disaster to resume business. It is feared that such a situation will lead to imitation in the future, and it will not only be the landlord's family who will do so. It is reasonable to prepare a document and submit it to your government for review, and for all the newly built houses that have been destroyed in the war zone, fair and appropriate measures should be stipulated for the lease, and proper crackdowns should be carried out, so that the survivors after the disaster can have a chance to rest, which is really convenient for the public.

Shipping Guild Telegraphs the Executive Yuan

Request to Reduce Vessel Registration Fees 174

The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association, for requesting a reduction in the registration fees for newly purchased vessels and exemption from mortgage registration fees, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Communications yesterday, saying: To the esteemed Executive Yuan in Nanjing, based on the joint statement of the member companies, in accordance with the provisions of the Vessel Registration Law, all shipping merchants, regardless of whether they are newly built or purchased vessels, must pay a registration fee of 4 per mille of the vessel's value according to Article 62, Paragraph 3. Furthermore, if the vessel is mortgaged, a registration fee of 2 per mille of the debt amount must be paid according to Paragraph 5 of the same article. Both burdens are excessively heavy. It is found that the shipping industry is a tool for foreign commercial warfare and maintaining transportation, and its rise and fall are related to international prestige. Therefore, all countries in the world take encouragement and maintenance as their purpose, either lending huge sums or providing appropriate subsidies. Seeing the persistence of the great powers in maintaining our country's shipping rights and their unwillingness to relax, the importance of the relationship is already known. Our country's commercial shipping, restricted by unequal treaties, is extremely immature. In order to meet the needs of resisting foreign vessels and preparing for the recovery of shipping rights, it is necessary to gradually add considerable vessels. Therefore, the Maintenance of Shipping Industry Law has special provisions, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications have repeatedly ordered to plan and prepare. At present, the number of heavy-tonnage vessels added by Chinese merchants is increasing day by day. Now that gold is expensive and silver is cheap, the purchase price is high. It is already extremely difficult to raise the vessel price. However, the registration fee must be paid at 4 per mille of the vessel's value, and the burden is so heavy that it is no different from blocking the path for Chinese people to raise funds to purchase vessels, which is contrary to the purpose of maintenance, encouragement, promotion, and preparation. This is one. The financial situation of shipping merchants is extremely difficult, which is known to all and cannot be concealed. It was already foreseen early on. Although we had repeatedly appealed last year, and your esteemed Yuan had approved the issuance of 10 million yuan of public bonds to maintain the shipping industry, the Ministry of Finance has not yet faithfully implemented it. Like quenching thirst with plums, we are eagerly waiting. Unexpectedly, natural disasters and foreign troubles have repeatedly multiplied, and the decline in the shipping merchants' business and the magnitude of the losses are unprecedented. It is inevitable that they will go bankrupt. Therefore, they have to bow their heads and swallow their voices, asking people to intercede and borrowing money to finance the vessels, which is increasing day by day. The matter is out of necessity, and the situation is very pitiful. However, the mortgage registration requires paying a registration fee of 2 per mille of the debt amount, which is no different from adding another blow to those who are drinking poison to quench their thirst. Moreover, during the era when the customs office was in charge of shipping administration, no fees were charged for the registration of vessel mortgages. It is true that all countries have no precedent for this. Therefore, the foreign customs officers followed the good laws of their own country to benefit the shipping merchants. Now that the person in charge has changed, the burden has actually increased. In the future, compared to the past, it will not only make people sigh that they are better here than there, but it will also be ridiculed for being contrary to the law on maintaining the shipping industry. This is two. The association is a shipping merchant organization. For all sufferings, we have no choice but to appeal on their behalf, and as fellow citizens, we have the obligation to state the facts. Therefore, we urgently request your esteemed Yuan to uphold the law on maintaining the shipping industry and the original intention of maintaining commercial shipping, and to order the Ministry of Communications to instruct all shipping administrations to reduce the fee for the registration of newly built or purchased vessels to 2 per mille of the vessel's value, and to exempt the fee for the registration of vessel mortgages, or to charge the fee according to the temporary registration example, in order to show promotion and support. Shipping rights are fortunate, and the shipping industry is fortunate. We urgently await your orders, Shanghai Shipping Industry Association, Chairman Yu Hede bows, Qi.

Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Still Handled by the Ministry 176

Jiangsu Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau Order No. 86 states: Based on the telegram from the Ministry of Finance's Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Division, we have read the telegram with respect. We have checked the case of the Jiangsu tobacco and alcohol license tax. Previously, the Jiangsu Provincial Government had requested in the Tanri telegram to directly reorganize it, and on the same day, we ordered the Finance Department to send personnel to various counties to collect the tax and directly deposit it into the provincial treasury. The Ministry found that the license tax has always been collected directly by the central government, and all provinces have followed it uniformly. Moreover, Article 1 of the Business Tax Law promulgated by the National Government also clearly stipulates that it is a central collection, and it is closely related to the reorganization of the tobacco and alcohol production and sales tax. It is difficult to divide it. The Ministry has previously replied to the Yangri telegram to cancel the original proposal in order to avoid disputes and has also presented a petition to the Executive Yuan to order a prohibition. Based on the previous situation, we must immediately instruct all the relevant license tax sub-bureaus to continue to handle the matter as before, to conduct thorough inspections, and to comply with the original plan. This is extremely important. In response to this, we checked the newspapers and, based on the reports submitted by the various tobacco and alcohol license tax sub-bureaus, we telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to inform the Jiangsu Provincial Government to cancel the previous order. On the one hand, we instructed the sub-bureaus to inform the tobacco and alcohol merchants to collect and pay taxes as usual. Now, based on the previous reasons, in addition to issuing it separately, we hereby order the sub-bureaus to comply with the processing of the farmland, and this order is urgent.

Joint Meeting of the Bean and Rice Industry Associations 177

The Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association convened a joint meeting of the northern and southern industries at the Cuixiu Hall in the Yimiao Temple yesterday afternoon to discuss the following important proposals: (1) The method for settling outstanding accounts in the northern and southern rice industries. British Assessor Continues Hearing of Haddon Estate Case 180

The Haddon estate case resumed yesterday morning at the British Consular Court. First, a Jewish legal expert explained Jewish law. If

after a Jew dies, he leaves his property to his wife or one of his children, then the inheritor is only considered a guardian of the family's interests. Furthermore, if a Jew marries a non-Jew, it is not recognized by law. instructing her to leave Shanghai. When the court convened in the afternoon, the testimony focused on the religious status of Haddon and his wife and their marriage.

Aftermath of Newspaper Workers' Strike Yesterday's Report 181

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Arrested More Than Twenty Workers

An Important Meeting Was Held the Night Before, and the Situation Was Very Serious

The Newspaper Workers' Union issued a message stating that since the Shanghai newspaper industry declared a strike on the 1st of this month at the Shenxin Shishi Sanbao (Shen Bao, Xin Bao, Shishi Xin Bao) to support the workers of the Shishi Xin Bao who were forced to leave the newspaper, Mr. Du Yuesheng came forward to mediate. The union, considering the good intentions of the third party and the importance of social news, agreed to the Shenxin Shishi Sanbao resuming work first. The issue of the Shishi Xin Bao firing workers

Mr. Du was responsible for negotiating, as detailed in the previous report. As of the day before yesterday, when there were still no concrete results, suddenly at 6:00 pm on the day before yesterday (the 8th), the Shishi Xin Bao management instigated the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team to send a large number of detectives to the union's headquarters, arresting more than twenty workers of the Shishi Xin Bao who had been fired, and destroying all the union's equipment and belongings. After the union heard about this, it convened an emergency meeting on the night of the 8th. Everyone said that the Shishi Xin Bao management had fired the workers, and after two months, there had been no results. The workers had suffered the pain of unemployment, and now they were suffering this unwarranted disaster. The Shishi Xin Bao management was really too cruel. The emotions were aroused, and the situation was tense. Several concrete measures were discussed and decided (temporarily not announced). Yesterday (the 9th), the union immediately sent representatives with a petition to the Municipal Government's Social Bureau and the Municipal Party Headquarters, demanding the release of the arrested workers and the thorough investigation of the person who instigated the destruction. At the same time, they went to the offices of He Xiangning, a member of the Central Committee, and Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan,

Petitioning to find a way to release the arrested workers. The results were all promising releases. Yesterday, the union also issued the following declaration: Compatriots, working brothers, since our Newspaper Workers' Union was openly destroyed and oppressed by the capitalists of the Shishi Xin Bao, the wounds and pain we have suffered are truly countless. However, in order to uphold justice and fairness, and in order to protect our own vital interests, even if we have to sacrifice everything, we will still resist them resolutely and will never retreat. On April 2, the Shishi Xin Bao capitalists

forced the workers to print the Da Wan Bao, causing a conflict that led to the dismissal of all the workers. This, on the part of the capitalists, is a kind of politically provocative method.

Therefore, there were thorough preparations in advance and proper arrangements afterwards, causing dozens of workers to suffer unemployment and the entire organization to be destroyed. Afterwards, despite our repeated negotiations and the efforts of various unions to help, the Shishi Xin Bao authorities did not retreat in the slightest. In their consistent strategy, it is very clear that they will never stop until they destroy our entire union organization. Therefore, in order to protect ourselves, we had this alliance strike on June 1st. After the strike,

Mr. Du Yuesheng came out to mediate. At that time, we also recognized Mr. Du's good-faith mediation and unanimously resumed work. However, how could we know that our resumption of work was originally to prevent the unrest from expanding, but the Shishi Xin Bao capitalists, seeing that we had already resumed work, not only insisted on their original strategy of destroying us, but also intensified their efforts. On the one hand, they falsely accused some workers who were working of being troublemakers and colluded with the patrol house to arrest them. On the other hand, they joined forces with the Public Security Bureau and sent a large number of armed detectives to the union's headquarters at 6:00 pm on the day before yesterday (the 8th). Without asking the reasons, they arrested all twenty-two workers of the Shishi Xin Bao who had been forced to leave the newspaper, including Wang Ke Gang, and destroyed all the arrangements in the union. This kind of unreasonable and violent act was openly staged in Shanghai in broad daylight, and it was carried out by the Chinese authorities. It is so painful and indignant for us to say it. Thinking about the distant and recent causes of this labor unrest, it was entirely created by the Shishi Xin Bao authorities. In order to protect ourselves, we had no choice but to resort to this final measure. The Shishi Xin Bao capitalists did not hesitate to attack us again and again. We are at a critical juncture of life and death. If the authorities still favor the Shishi Xin Bao, abuse their power, and destroy the labor movement, then we will only use all our strength to fight them in a final battle. Compatriots, workers, we have been oppressed and can no longer tolerate it. In order to survive, we have no choice but to embark on the road of struggle. We hope that we will be given strong assistance in this struggle. Shanghai Newspaper Workers' Union, June 9th.

Time flies, and it has been two years. Commander Liang has strict discipline in governing the army, which is admired by everyone. Last autumn, the troops stationed in Huai'an built dams to prevent floods, and the people of Dadian were especially grateful. However, it has recently been heard that the troops stationed in various counties often set up inspection offices to collect opium losses. As a result, local hoodlums take advantage of the name to extort money and distribute opium soil and red and white pills. Or it is said that because the defense area is vast and the people are uneven, it is difficult to ensure that there are no a few officers and adjutants who are negligent for a while and collude with petty people, which leads to the violation of the law and conscience. If so, then they are a scourge and tarnish the reputation of the national army, and should be given appropriate punishment to serve as a warning. Or it is said that the 25th Route Army, because the government's military pay cannot be issued on time, and the hungry army is waiting for food, it is urgent to set up a levy. This statement is not true and we dare not know, but according to common sense, the government takes taxes from the people to meet the national needs, and the needs of the national army should be taken from the national treasury. The budget is listed in the book, and all are aware of it. If the government's military pay is short, and the garrison is allowed to raise funds on the spot without limitation, the people's pain will be deeper, and the national discipline will be worse. What kind of governance system will it become? It is enough to make this kind of speculation unworthy of deep belief. However, it is believed that various counties in northern Jiangsu suffered unprecedented floods last year, and the land is full of devastation. This spring, it has been indirectly affected by the war and is even more exhausted. How should the government entrusted by our people and the national defense army directly under the government be merciful to the dying and helpless people? It is inappropriate to ignore them, and how can we bear to trample them? The 25th Route Army is stationed in various counties in northern Jiangsu. Are there any offices set up to collect donations? Is the government's military pay not being issued on time? And how many months are needed for the officers and soldiers of the 25th Route Army? How much is the pay needed? The people of Jiangsu have suffered greatly, and the doubts are not resolved. We dare to drink tears and blood, regardless of death, and beg the public officials of the esteemed government to grant a thorough investigation and a clear declaration, so that our dying people

know clearly where the truth lies, so that even if they encounter misfortune, wait for rescue indefinitely, and have no way to save themselves, they will be fortunate to know the reason for their death, and death may be relieved. Now, the China Economic Society's Shanghai Branch is compiling a "China-Japan Trade Research Institute Work Manual", which contains a rich collection of content and accurate research. It is the most valuable masterpiece for studying Sino-Japanese business. It will be published soon. Among them, the "National Goods Trademark" item plans to search for the names and patterns of national goods trademarks in order to compare and refer to foreign goods trademarks. This matter concerns industrial and commercial interests, and it is specially notified to all industrial and commercial industries in this port and other ports. Please submit the names, patterns, and products used for national goods trademarks, as well as the status of registration, in detail within five days to the "National Goods Trademark Collection Office, Shanghai Beile Road Mechanical Federation". Please send the industries in other ports to the conference within ten days for forwarding, so that you will not look forward and miss the opportunity. I am very grateful for this special notice to all industries and factories in this port and other ports.

The case has been informed, and the Shanghai Municipal Government has been consulted to transfer the Social Bureau to find out the truth and handle it impartially. You should wait for the approval. According to this approval, the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau has sent personnel to the General Association and the company to investigate and found that it is not appropriate to violate the contract and reduce salaries.

Guns and Ammunition Vanish Without a Trace 188

Gao Qianlong Reports Theft

Gatekeepers All Deny Involvement

Gao Qianlong, a 40-year-old Ningbo native who runs a small teahouse at 15 Guoxiang Lane, Hengtong Road, Zhabei, went to the Second Section of the Fourth District of the Public Security Bureau, Qiuan Lane Police Station (formerly the original location of the Second Section of the Fourth District) yesterday at around 11:00 AM to report that when the Japanese troops ravaged Zhabei the other day and the 19th Route Army retreated to the second line of defense, a patrolman surnamed Chen left a rifle and a pistol, along with more than ten rows of bullets, at his shop. Fearing that the Japanese soldiers would find out and it would be detrimental to him, he hid the rifle inside the roof tiles and the pistol and bullets in the ditch at the entrance. At the time, only Xu Renhuai, Wu Jiuguan, patrolmen working as gatekeepers in a certain concession, and Lu Zixi, the gatekeeper in Guoxiang Lane, saw it. Now, all the firearms and ammunition have disappeared. He suspects they were stolen by Xu and the other two. After receiving the report, the police station dispatched several officers led by Police Chief Cai to arrest Xu, Wu, and Lu. After a brief interrogation at the station, they were sent to the Second Section. According to the plaintiff's statement to Section Chief Han Tiexian, it was roughly as described above. However, the defendant Xu Renhuai, 39 years old, from Yancheng, and Wu Jiuguan, also 39 years old, from Ningbo, and Lu Zixi, 62 years old, from Haimen, all claimed that Gao Qianlong was making a false accusation out of spite and denied stealing the guns and ammunition. After reviewing the statements, the section chief deemed the case important and ordered them to be transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further interrogation.

Li Zhixiang Transferred to Water Police for Investigation 189

Li Zhixiang, also known as Li Lipi, a robber from Hunan province, 31 years old, colluded with others in April of this year to rob passengers of their belongings on a small steamboat in Paotaiwan, Wujiang County, using weapons and kidnapping 23 hostages. During the pursuit by government police, he opened fire and killed three officers. On April 21st, he robbed a Shengze bus steamboat with his gang, kidnapped hostages, and fled to Shanghai. The Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police issued a wanted notice and sent Detective Wan Zhinan to Shanghai to conduct a secret investigation. On the 8th (the day before yesterday) at 1:00 PM, Li was spotted by Detective Wan as he was passing the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Shangxian Lane in the French Concession. Wan immediately called for Officer No. 101 and arrested Li, taking him to the police station for detention. Yesterday, he was transferred to the Second Special Court. At 2:00 PM, Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the trial in the First Criminal Court. First, the police lawyer Gu Shouxi explained the case, stating that the defendant had colluded with others to commit robbery in the interior, robbing a small boat, kidnapping people, resisting arrest, and killing government officials. The Water Police had sent a detective to Shanghai to arrest the defendant and hand him over. The police station did not object to the transfer. Detective Wan Zhinan of the Public Security Bureau also submitted an official document stating the case and requesting permission to transfer the case for investigation. The defendant's statement was evasive. After reviewing the statements, Judge Xiong ruled that Li Zhixiang should be handed over to the Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Department detectives to be taken back for investigation.

Yu Shengshan Blames It on Lies

Yu Shengshan from Liuhe and Li Zicai from Wuxi wrote threatening letters between May 21st and June 1st and delivered them to Hu Yueshan, the owner of Xintai (i.e., Xintai Electrical Materials Factory) at 210 Glen Road, Yangshupu, extorting 10,000 yuan, claiming to be the Preparatory Office for the Southeast Self-Defense Army. It was written by someone surnamed Jia who set up a fortune-telling stall on Dagu Road. The draft was written by the defendant Li Zicai. He then submitted the letter for inspection. The plaintiff Hu Yueshan claimed that he did not know either of the defendants. He received the threatening letter on the 27th of last month. The next morning, he reported it to the police station. The police station then dispatched Qian Wancai and a police detective to the designated meeting place. He did not go with them. Qian Wancai then stated that he was waiting near the Xietu Road bridge when the defendant Yu San Yi arrived. He spoke with him. Yu said, "How much money did you bring today?" Qian told him that they had to negotiate before arranging a place to hand over the money. He was then arrested by the police detective. When questioned, Yu Shengshan completely denied his previous admission that he conspired with Li Zicai, directed him to go to the meeting place to receive the money, and his statements to the police station, claiming that they were all lies and not voluntary. Li

Zicai also denied it and hired lawyer Lin Yingqing to defend him. Judge Qiao ordered them to be remanded in custody for further investigation.

Suicide

Question of Name and Handwriting 191

Jiang Yusheng Confirms Identity as Son and Claims Body

On the evening of the 7th of this month at 7:00 PM, Yao Guanfeng (i.e., Jiang Guifang), a 19-year-old from Huzhou, went to the Tongfa Inn on Qipu Road alone. After booking Room 5, he took poison. The next morning, Zhao Afu, a tea server at the inn, discovered him and reported it to the accounting office, which then reported it to the Hui Si police station, ordering detectives to investigate. A suicide note was found near his body, stating that he was tired of life due to prolonged unemployment and financial difficulties. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment but died. The body was taken to the forensic examination office on Faelun Road. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor appointed by the First Special District Court, along with forensic doctor Wei Ligong, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, arrived at the office. They determined that the body was placed in a public space. Zhao Afu stated that after the deceased booked the room, he asked him to make tea and then went to sleep. The next morning, at around 11:00 AM, he went to wake him up and saw him moaning in bed. He then reported it to the accounting office. Jiang Yusheng, 46 years old, a silk merchant living at 17 Rehe Road, stated that the deceased was indeed his son. The name Yao Guanfeng was a pseudonym. His real name was Jiang Guifang. He could not determine if the handwriting on the letter was his because he was often away from home. Guo concluded that the deceased Jiang Guifang had indeed died from poisoning himself before his death. The body was handed over to his father, Jiang Yusheng, to arrange for the coffin and burial.

People in Pudong Are Buzzing

Brothers Kill Older Brother

Zhang Linsheng, the deceased horse racing head from Huayuanshi Bridge, Pudong, was involved in a property dispute, leading to internal strife. Zhang’s third son, Zhang Qingxiang, and his maternal uncle, Zhang Quansheng, shot and killed his older brother, Zhang Yuxiang, and his half-brother, Zhang Guoxiang. According to Gu Chenshi, Zhang Qingxiang came to look for Guoxiang around 5:00 PM before the incident, but did not meet him and left. According to Zhang Achuan, who lived in the same house as Gu Chenshi, her testimony was similar. According to Lu Dingshi, a tenant of Gu Chenshi, her testimony was the same. The security chief Xie Along stated that he reported the examination of the case, but the details were not clear. Zhu Shangzhi, the platoon leader of the Tangqiao Security Regiment, now a squad leader, stated that Zhang Quansheng was formerly a member of the team. He did not actually understand what happened after Zhang Yuxiang was killed, but people were buzzing, saying that the brothers killed their older brother. Zhang Qingxiang's witness Sheng Jinsheng stated that he got married recently. On the day of the incident, September 22nd of last year, Zhang Qingxiang, Zhu Jinlong, and Zhang Liugen came to his house at around 8:00 AM and played mahjong until around 4:00 PM. Qingxiang's mother-in-law came to call him and told him not to gamble. At that time, there were still two rounds of mahjong, so they dispersed at around 5:00 PM. He did not know where Qingxiang went, but he saw him heading south. He did not ask him. They did not know his mother-in-law and did not know how she got to his house. Zhu Jinlong and Zhang Liugen gave similar testimony, but said that Zhang Qingxiang's mother-in-law came at 5:00 PM and called him for dinner, and did not say anything else.

There were only two decks of cards, etc. Qiu Asong, the security chief of the 16th map of Tangqiao, stated that on September 22nd, Zhang Quansheng had a dispute with a neighbor over land rent, which he mediated. He and Yan Zilin left together in the evening, and he left first. Chen Kunlin stated that he lived next door to Zhang Quansheng. On September 22nd, he saw Quansheng and Yan Zilin eating dinner and washing their faces. Zhang Quansheng's wife, Shen, said that after her husband was arrested, she hid the pistol in the stove out of fear. Unexpectedly, the stepdaughter burned it while cooking. Later, the stepdaughter buried it in the ashes. She did not know the stepdaughter's name. At this point, the official said that the case was generally clear and agreed to the lawyer's request to schedule a debate.
