Incoming Correspondence

Dong Xiujia's Draft

Three-Year Construction Plan for Jiangsu Province 205

I believe that the Premier's (Sun Yat-Sen's) teachings emphasize construction above all else. Since the founding of the Party-State, the National Construction Commission at the national level, the Construction Department at the provincial level, the Public Works Bureau at the municipal level, and the Construction Bureau at the county level have all been responsible for striving to make progress, striving to fulfill the Premier's grand vision of "everyone makes the most of their talent, every piece of land makes the most of its value, every object makes the most of its use, and every commodity flows smoothly." Jiangsu Province protects the capital (Nanjing) and borders Shanghai, acting as a national hub for transportation. It is not only a political center and a commercial hub, but also has developed agriculture and industry. Academia is also prosperous. The climate is suitable, the scenery is beautiful, and the humanities and geography are renowned in the Southeast. In terms of construction, it is more urgent than other provinces. The Construction Department of this province has been established for five years, and has had several leaders, all of whom have made remarkable achievements. My (Dong Xiujia's) knowledge and experience are far inferior to those of my predecessors, but I was mistakenly entrusted with serving my hometown. I will encourage each other in our hometown to maintain our integrity, follow the old rules, and be diligent and careful for the past four months. However, the country is currently in a difficult situation, and the province's finances have been severely affected, almost reaching exhaustion. Furthermore, after the floods, the Yun embankments, sea dikes, and embankments of dozens of counties collapsed at the same time, all of which need to be repaired in a timely manner. In addition, due to the importance of national defense, military roads and telecommunications projects in various places must also be completed on schedule. All of these must be done simultaneously in the shortest possible time. However, while it is difficult to pre-determine a direction for temporary work, daily progress cannot be without a procedure. It should be noted that the period of tutelage is expected to last for six years,

More than half of which has now passed, leaving only the last three years to plan for construction. The overall facilities are urgent and busy, and it is well known that completion is not easy. However, in the face of difficulties, if there is no spirit of struggling to achieve success, it seems to be losing the original purpose of construction. Based on what the Construction Department is responsible for, such as water conservancy, highways, telecommunications, navigation, municipal administration, and provincial capital construction, there are six major points. To enumerate their details,

The management of the Yun River, dredging ports, repairing rivers, building embankments, dike construction,  construction, pond construction, and gate construction all belong to water conservancy. Roadbed, pavement, bridges, culverts, land acquisition, price payment, relocation, compensation, all belong to highways. Provincial long-distance telephone, provincial automatic telephone, provincial radio stations, broadcasting equipment, and the management of various privately-run electrical businesses, all belong to telecommunications. Suppressing inland river shipping, reorganizing river traffic,

All belong to navigation. Reorganizing the streets of all counties, opening parks in all counties, suppressing municipal buildings, adding artesian wells in various places, managing merchant vegetable farms in all counties, and facilitating human-powered vehicles all belong to municipal administration.

As for prospering the provincial capital, repairing roads and bridges, reorganizing vehicle traffic, planning and building Xiangshan port, embellishing urban and rural scenery, and building public housing, all belong to provincial capital construction. All of the above are under the scope of our responsibility. If we want to implement these policies effectively, we must first have a meticulous plan, a sequence of priorities, and a predetermined timetable. Otherwise, those involved will lose their bearings, and those outside will be unable to understand what is going on. This is why the Construction Department's three-year plan must be disclosed in advance so that we can urge progress on schedule. In order to plan for future facilities, review past history, and perceive the difficulties of progress, there are further remarks that I hope people from all over the country will understand. Since the establishment of the Construction Department, the heads of the department have changed several times, and the organization has been repeatedly

changed. Previously, the water conservancy organs originally had the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Office, located in Yangzhou, engaged in canal work, and the province set up a Water Conservancy Bureau to supervise it. In the spring of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), the Yangzhou Engineering Office was merged into the Water Conservancy Bureau. After the floods, a portion was split off from the Water Conservancy Bureau to form the Jiangbei Canal Closure Engineering Office. In the winter of that year, the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Aftermath Committee was established. Regarding sea dikes, there was originally the Jiangnan Sea Dike Office, which was later abolished and divided into Baotai Song three counties, with the heads of the Construction Bureaus of the three counties concurrently holding responsibility. Recently, the Jiangnan Dike Engineering Aftermath Committee was jointly formed by the province and the city. This is the situation regarding the organizational changes of the Water Conservancy Bureau. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Two-One Branch Talk

Is It Western Goods? 206

— Shan Liao

! The weather is getting warmer, and summer clothes must be prepared; the material for summer clothes must be domestic goods, otherwise, it will be Western goods; nothing else will be bought; if bought, it will be a traitor!

This is the determination of patriotic youths when buying clothing materials.

! Alas! The price of this cloth from Wan Zai is too expensive. At eighty-five cents per foot, wouldn't I buy spun silk? That one, rough and yellow, also costs thirty-five cents per foot, and it doesn't look very nice on.

This is the patriotic youth talking to himself in the cloth store.

! Sir, buy muslin; it is fine, clean, and white, looks nice, and the price is very reasonable, less than thirty cents per foot.

Isn't muslin a product of Japan?

! No, sir, the muslin in this store is a Western product. Look! Fine or not fine, clean or not clean?

! Indeed, cut me thirty-six feet; although I am cutting it, I still have some doubts as to whether it is Western goods!

! Sir, don't worry.

When the shop assistant said "don't worry," thirty-six feet of muslin had already been cut; after collecting the money and folding the muslin, the patriotic youth carried this package of muslin, walking and thinking:

! This muslin is Western goods, so is it that cheap?

After walking a little further, he comforted himself,

! If you want it to be beautiful and cheap, whether it's Western goods or not, you can only go with the flow.

War Zone Sketch II 207

— Qian Taisheng

丨From Baoshan Road to Fort Taiwan

The second day after the opening of the Songhu branch line was a Sunday, so I decided to go to Fort Taiwan.

The car started from Baoshan Road, and to the north was the ruined and scorched Baoshan Road. When the car passed each destroyed house, it was truly unbearable to look at! Imagine the raging fire, imagine the fellow villagers, young and old, escaping from the bullets, with death chasing after them, their homes burned in the fire. 1932 was truly not a peaceful year.

The car stopped at Tiantong Nunnery. Japanese troops were still stationed there, which was truly stimulating. All the way to Jiangwan, all the schools and factories were destroyed. From the car, you could see schools such as Labor University, Law School, and Patriotic School, all dilapidated and collapsed in this countryside of fluttering butterflies and blooming wildflowers. Most of the factories were beyond recovery!

After passing Gaojing Temple, we arrived at Zhanghuabang, beyond which was Wenzaobang. The car stopped there as the terminal, no longer going further.

From the station, you could see the rising sun flag flying over the Japanese-owned Huari Yarn Factory, where it was said that troops were still stationed.

Walking along the outer road of Wenzaobang, we arrived at Wusong Town, which had been completely destroyed, and passed the so-called "Shirakawa Bridge" and "Kanazawa Bridge" named by the Japanese. There were temporary shops set up on the road for business, probably by the merchants of Wusong Town. However, Wusong Town, which was gradually prospering, had also suffered this great calamity.

Maintaining order on the road were the so-called "Special Police" from Beiping. From a distance, seeing their white leggings, I thought they were foreign police.

In general, Wenzaobang and Wusong Town were completely destroyed.

Walking from the end of Wusong Town, we arrived at Fort Taiwan. I then turned north along Zhonggong Road to see the China Public School, which I had heard was destroyed.

Except for the science building, which had just been completed, facing south and hit by a single shell, the rest was still intact and could be repaired. However, the clock tower, library, auditorium, old dormitories, and the three-story new dormitory on the east side, built by the school's former president Ma Junwu, were completely destroyed. Two faculty dormitories in the southeast corner were hit by a single shell, but the rest was fine. To restore the school to its original state, it would probably take at least four or five hundred thousand yuan.

After leaving China Public School, we went to the North and South Forts.

It was as lively as visiting historical sites and scenic spots. The road to the fort was too crowded. Women in their early summer attire, sitting in resilient, gasoline-burning motorcars, drove up the muddy paths to the fort, which was previously considered forbidden territory. Climbing up the fort, the vast expanse of gurgling river water, the twenty-four foreign warships and countless planes bombarding this defenseless old fort, how could the brave troops continue to defend it?

The muddied Yellow River, stained with blood, flowed endlessly, shedding silent tears, sighing silently towards the visiting people. It flowed away with such longing, looking at the dozens of destroyed steel cannons, large and small.

Before, behind, left, and right of the fort were huge craters caused by aircraft bombs. The cement-poured gun emplacements were also shattered. Scattered shells still lay on the edges of the destroyed steel cannons. The fort, stained with hot blood, and the gurgling river water, would probably not be easily washed clean.

Trivial Talk 208

— Fei Wenbao

Chinese people have always prided themselves on being seven feet tall. They often regard their eastern neighbors as short and ugly. Before September 18th, I observed the Japanese people I knew. I felt that only about 30% were short. The rest were similar to our Chinese people. It is said that since the Russo-Japanese War, the average height of their people has increased by about two inches. Now it has increased to four inches. When asked why, they said:

"It's due to dedicated exercise." The English are originally a Saxon race. Most of the people are short and fat. Therefore, they are called John Bull. However, through diligent exercise for more than a hundred years, they are now tall, healthy, and beautiful. Our country lags behind others in everything. Only in eating and foot-binding are we famous in the world. However, the race we produce is also becoming increasingly degenerate. There is even the insult of "Sick Man of East Asia." Reading about the survival of the fittest, and considering the future of the nation, I cannot help but feel emotional.

Marriage and Divorce 209

— Qian

Now is an era of freedom. What young people generally like to say is "freedom" and "love." Therefore, the freedom of marriage has also greatly increased. However, as marriage has become freer, the number of divorces has also increased at the same time. What is the reason for this? Of course, there are many examples of divorce that are unavoidable and out of helplessness. However, based on my observation, there are special reasons for generally marrying freely and then divorcing.

First, being a lover is easy. Being able to cry, laugh, and dress up is enough. But being a wife is very difficult. Before marriage, the husband sees you as a capable, articulate, and educated woman. But after marriage, you are not good at serving your husband and in-laws, and you are lazy. This is naturally inappropriate. So the first reason for divorce is a lack of cultivation.

Second, young people's minds are fickle. Today they read romance novels, tomorrow they watch love movies. True.

On Saving the Nation Through Thrift and Frugality (7) 210

— Narrated by Nie Zengjifen, written by her son Qijie

Indeed, carnal desires are all petty stirrings of selfishness, and are as incompatible with public morality as water and fire. Only by overcoming personal desires can any construction be hoped for. As Wang Yangming said, "It is easy to kill bandits in the mountains, but difficult to kill the bandits in the heart." Being able to overcome the enemy in one's heart is what it means to conquer oneself and strengthen oneself. In addition to the politicians mentioned above, great thinkers such as Rousseau, Tolstoy, and Marx, Kropotkin, were all able to reject material

enjoyment and live a life of frugality and simplicity. Rousseau and Tolstoy both abstained from meat. (Kropotkin also seemed to be a vegetarian.) And in modern times, the great scientist Edison, in his diet and daily life, was always in the laboratory. He had no interest in worldly pleasures. The two giants of the automobile industry, Ford and Sloan, neither smoked nor drank, nor did they like entertainment. The great scientist Einstein was simple and humble, with no desire for profit. A film company invited him to speak on screen for a fee of two hundred thousand US dollars. Einstein declined, saying that knowledge was not for money. Many other famous scientists have similar integrity. Their academic

achievements were never intended for carnal enjoyment. Therefore, it cannot be said that there is invention only after desire. On the contrary. Great inventors and thinkers who are driven by lust have never been heard of. Therefore, recent people say that developing desires promotes science and culture is purely speculation. It cannot be proven by facts. It is only used to justify their faults. Looking for counter-evidence, in Chinese and foreign history, any era that goes from stability to destruction is the result of the development of desires. The facts are clear and countless. Even the recent great war in Europe, the current precarious situation of countries holding each other in check, and the internal conflicts in our country for the past twenty years, are all manifestations of the development of desires. The degree of destruction is extremely tragic. The ingenious inventions produced are also nothing but for destruction and deceit. Have desires ever contributed to the evolution of the world?

It's fun to do the same thing. As a result, they often develop a feeling of boredom with their husband or wife. All they want to do is pursue the empty, illusory romance in novels. As a result, some unfortunate events occur. So the second reason for divorce is a lack of responsibility.

Third, the current social environment is really too bad. Young people's strange and outlandish attire, extravagant and licentious behavior, all have a bad influence. We often see, and even among so-called university students, they will write letters to women they barely know, saying things like "I admire your scholarship!" "Your letters are so well written!" "I hope we can be friends. Is that okay?" "Let's just be literary friends." These letters are sent out casually. It doesn't matter if they have a spouse or if the other person has a spouse. As a result, those with weak wills will inevitably give up on themselves. So the third reason for divorce is a bad environment.

If young people can pay attention to these three reasons and take precautions, it may be of some help to marital happiness.

Record of the Guanghan Palace 211

— Suicheng

In the western suburbs of Luoyang, there is a military camp called West Palace, which was built by Yuan Shikai in his day. Later, General Wu Ziyu stationed troops there and rebuilt it. Guanghan Palace is one of them. Its structure is very ordinary, but its style is unique. At the entrance, there is a path like a team, from top to bottom, a total of thirty-three steps. At the end of the steps, there is another door. Entering again is the auditorium. Therefore, although the exterior is low, once inside, it feels surprisingly high. There are eight or nine caves around, deep and dark and unfathomable. Peeking into them, one feels a chilling coldness and dares not enter. It is said that there were no caves originally. They were dug in the seventeenth year of the Republic. At that time, the Northern Expeditionary Army advanced to Henan and was about to approach Luoyang at any moment. Airplanes came to drop bombs from time to time. General Wu was worried about this, so he opened up many caves to discuss matters with his colleagues and to avoid bombs. Since the National Crisis Conference used this as a meeting place, it was sealed with mud. Only three small holes were left at the door, with gas lamps lit inside, as a place for members to rest and drink tea. There are no other rooms inside, so it was used in this way.

Above the main door, there was originally the inscription "Guanghan," which was more than a foot in size, written by Kang Youwei. The brushwork was vigorous. Later, the

Central Party Headquarters changed the place to the Central Auditorium and ordered the plasterers to chisel it off. Those who come later will no longer know that there was such a thing as Guanghan.

Brief News: Yu Yifen is a talented student of Hanyun and his calligraphy is very similar to his teacher. He is currently working with others to sell fans and is well-regarded in the art world. Now he has independently completed one hundred leaves of small regular script fan heads, each priced at two yuan. It is also possible to add a signature on request. Contact address: No. 61, Hehe Lane, Lufei Road, Shanghai

Memoirs of a Double Life in the Military (74) 212

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Nine: Attending a Special Train, a False Alarm; Sitting in a Cold Office, a Distant Dream

An Yutian wanted to move to the train window, open the curtains, and peek outside. However, this side did not face the platform. He had to open the carriage door and go out to see it from the train window on that side of the aisle. Unfortunately, the mechanism on this carriage door was in disrepair due to military use and had a problem. Just now, when Deputy Guo led him away, he had closed the door too forcefully, making it very tight. He could not pull it open quickly. Helpless, he slumped down again. The sound of military music and the commands of officers shouting "Salute!" rose into the air. It was obvious that Military Governor Ye had boarded the train. Then, in the aisle of this carriage, there was a series of sounds of leather boots stomping on the train floor. It seemed that many people had also run onto the train. Suddenly, the carriage door was pulled open violently from the outside, and four or five burly and imposing warriors from the guard team burst in. They carried hand-held automatic guns on their shoulders and countless small straight strips of bullet belts around their chests. Seeing An Yutian occupying a berth alone, they questioned him harshly, asking who he was. An Yutian hurriedly reported his official title of Counselor and explained that Deputy Guo had been ordered to entertain him. Among them was a burly man with a face full of menacing flesh and the most murderous aura. He still didn't believe it and spat in his face. Pointing his finger fiercely at his nose, he roared, "Don't talk nonsense. If you're a counselor, why aren't you wearing a badge? I know. You little bastard, you did a good job of working on Xiao Guo. He secretly brought you up here, but it's squeezing our berths." An Yutian realized that this warrior was scolding him for impersonating an official and sitting in the special train. He couldn't help but become furious. He wanted to clarify, but when he reached into his coat, a letter of appointment had already been given to Liang Xiaoyun. He couldn't produce any real evidence at this time. He wanted to wake up the Deputy Zhu above him to testify for him, but Deputy Zhu only cared about sleeping and refused to turn over. An Yutian was so anxious that his face turned red and his veins bulged. He walked angrily towards the outside, saying, "I just received the appointment today, so I didn't have time to get a badge. If you don't believe me, I'll leave. I still have my wife in the Fifth Madam's compartment. When I find Deputy Guo or Deputy Mao, I'm not afraid of not having a place to squat." At this time, the special train had started moving amidst the noise. An Yutian staggered a few steps. The warriors suddenly chased after him and dragged him back, saying, "You, why are you so inconsiderate? There are assigned positions on this train. Can you just barge in here without a badge? I advise you to find less trouble. Just squat here honestly for a while."

Shen Bao Local Supplement June 10, 1932, Wednesday

(No Extra Charge)

Opinion

Urging the Retention of the 19th Route Army 213

— Buddha

Since the news of the 19th Route Army being transferred to Fujian to suppress the Communists spread, letters and telegrams have been exchanged, or representatives have been sent to urge their retention. Originally, the 19th Route Army sacrificed themselves for the country, were loyal and brave in resisting the enemy, and should be sincerely retained to show respect. But my opinion is not so, for three reasons:

1. The Japanese troops are about to withdraw completely. Now that there is no resistance, there is no need to station troops there. This is the first reason.

2. The Communists are now very rampant and spreading widely. Regardless of their transfer or other reasons, suppressing the Communists is also a proper matter. This is the second reason.

3. Although the Japanese troops are about to withdraw completely, the number of our troops stationed along the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou lines is still quite large. With so many troops gathered, it is easy to cause misunderstandings and incidents.

A gentleman loves people with virtue, and can never abandon facts and act solely on emotions.

Science

Methods for Early Maturation of Vegetables and Fruits 216

— Qing

Vegetables and fruits are fresher and tastier when they are in season, and their selling price is higher, and buyers also welcome them. Therefore, gardeners and old farmers often try to improve their planting to produce mature vegetables and fruits in a short period of time, hoping to obtain thicker profits to cater to the psychology of buyers. Although they do not know scientific methods, when we look at them with a scientific eye, they sometimes fit scientific principles very well. Unfortunately, they lack a scientific foundation and deep theories to add to various researches to reach that mythical realm. Now I introduce a little method to them that they can get a kind of reference, and I think people who are interested in horticulture are very welcome.

Planting Method Using Electric Lights This method is to make vegetables and fruits and leaves and branches receive heat and light, and grow thick green leaves and lush fruits in a short period of time. His equipment is also very simple. He installs electric lights with stronger light in the greenhouse protecting vegetables and fruits, and it is better to hang a thermometer to test the temperature. A planter in Germany once discovered in his greenhouse protecting flowers that plants are heated and illuminated by electricity, and the flowers, fruits and branches and leaves can actually be large and good. We will definitely get good results if we try it according to the law.

Chemical Method This method was reported by Dr. Rob err Stewart, director of the Agricultural Science Department of Nafo University in the United States. He said that chemical methods can make immature fruits and vegetables mature early, and the aroma of fruits and vegetables does not change. He used canvas canopies to cover half of the fields, and then sprayed the vegetables in the canvas canopies with a chemical medicine made of alcohol and sulfuric acid called Ethylene. In less than a few days, the vegetables under the canvas have already grown vigorously and have matured, while the vegetables not covered by the canvas are still short and stunted and have not matured.

In another experiment, two unripe bananas were cut and hung on a shelf, one sprayed with Ethylene and one not. After forty-eight hours, the one sprayed with Ethylene had matured, and eating it had the same aroma as naturally matured, while the one not sprayed with chemicals was still green, hard and unripe. This method is also very easy to do. We only need to use alcohol and sulfuric acid to make Ethylene, and apply it to the vegetables as appropriate.

Family Problems

Talking About the Employer 217

— Wang Shibing

Next to the tiger stove is the place where Shanghai maids talk. When they meet their colleagues, they must talk a few words. The content of the conversation does not deviate from the three words (talking about the employer). Now I will record a few sentences of their conversation below.

A: "Sister, are you busy living in the × mansion? How much money do you earn a month?"

B: "Alas! Don't mention it. To others, it seems that our master is an official in the ×× government in Beiping, and there is only this × madam at home. Life must be very simple, and the madam must be very generous, so there must be some income. But I don't know that this madam has a very bad temper. She is very extravagant in making friends outside, but when it comes to treating the people in the mansion, she is very harsh! Only these five old ocean coins a month, and there is no extra income at all. Speaking of life, although the master is out, there is only one good person. You don't know that there are many good male and female friends, coming in and out every day, making my head hurt. These young masters and young ladies are all big shots, calling me alone, how can I serve them all? If there is something not taken care of, the madam will scold me. Recently, I have been interested in that foreign firm's little devil Xiao Wang. The two of them go dancing and watching movies every day, coming back in the middle of the night, and still asking for tea and water. Sister, do you think it's hard?"

A: "Oh! So that's how it is. Speaking of our place, the madam is still good, but there are only two young ladies. It's hard to say in a word. They dress up like demons every day, and they also dance and eat big meals. Their tempers are so bad, if something is wrong, they will scold people and beat people. Not to mention the little ones, who are beaten to a bloody mess. Even us maids are often scolded and get angry. Although they spend tens of dollars a day, they are not willing to spend a penny on us. They are very busy, with the eldest lady doing something and the second lady doing something, calling us non-stop. We eat well, but we don't even get the leftover rice. Alas! I don't want to work in such a family!"

C: "You two are still good. Like in our place, the employer is a young couple. The man works in a bank, and the young madam gambles at the ×× company every day. Recently, she has lost a lot. She tears down the house and pawns things at home. The young master finds out and investigates, but she says the maid stole it. I feel so wronged like this. It looks like I'm not happy to do it anymore!"

D: "Sisters, don't say anything. Eating this meal in Shanghai is the same everywhere. Which family is not snobbish? If you want to change employers, I don't think it will be as good, because these rich people are all domineering and think that they should treat servants like this. They don't know that the rich are also raised by mothers. Those who look for food are also raised by fathers and mothers. It's just that a few coins are wrong. Call your masters and madams, they are all people. It's really unforgivable to treat poor people like this. So I advise the two sisters, it's better to be familiar than to be unfamiliar. If you want to change, it's just changing the soup but not the medicine!"

Nonsense

Wind, Horse, and Ox 218

— Yun

Today I talked to A about the way to deal with the world, and I asked him for advice.

"The method of dealing with the world is actually very simple, and it can be summed up in the three characters "wind, horse, and ox", but it is really not easy to do!" He said.

"Doesn't "wind, horse, and ox" mean not asking about anything? That is becoming a hermit instead of entering the world."

"This "wind, horse, and ox" is not that "wind, horse, and ox"," he replied with a smile, "This means showing off, flattering, and bragging."

"Hey! I'm not going to be a small dog in the political arena," I asked strangely.

"Ha! Whether you enter the political world, the business world, fall in love, or want to be a scholar or celebrity, whatever, you always need this wind, horse, and ox. If you use it skillfully, you can get a beautiful wife, concubine, and a tall building. Otherwise, you will suffer for a lifetime. Wind, horse, and ox are like the gods of fate, holding the power of life and death. Don't take it too lightly."

Student Work

My Fellow Student's Thesis 219

A few days ago, at home, I saw a note left by my friend Wang Jun, knowing that he had something important to meet with me about, saying that he wanted me to write a graduation thesis. At the time I thought, "This is strange, a graduation thesis, what does this have to do with me? I am not a college student, and I don't need to graduate. . . ." Soon after, I forgot about it because of something. But I agreed to meet with Wang Jun.

Of course, today is Sunday, I have time, and I have to wait for Wang Jun at home as promised. When he arrived, it was not long after noon, and I was lazily sleeping in bed, resting my fatigue.

Because I haven't seen him for a whole year, I inevitably felt distant from his life situation. However, from his brand new white gabardine pants and blue-and-white striped flannel, and the neatness of his neatly ironed jacket, I could guess that his life must be beautiful, even more pleasant than before.

Sure enough, from his conversation, I learned that he was already a college student, and now he was approaching graduation, so the graduation thesis was very important to him.

"We have been friends for many years," Wang Jun said awkwardly, "so I think you will definitely help me with this thesis, and it doesn't need to be very good, just a thesis is enough."

"But I don't know what you are studying? Is it politics or economics?" I asked.

"No, I am studying Chinese studies."

"Oh? This is difficult. You know that I usually have no research on Chinese studies, and I have very few reference books myself, and the Oriental Library was burned by the Japanese, so how can this be successful?"

"No, I think you have written usually, as long as it hasn't been published, any kind will do."

"That won't work, sir! For example, you are studying Chinese studies, and if you take an economic thesis, can that also be done?" I smiled, repeatedly stating the reason why this cannot be mixed up, but he was still stubborn, still saying that as long as it is a thesis, and at the same time trying to cover up his difficulties in not being able to write, but I still couldn't obey, because this is too difficult. . . .

When I finally sent him out the door, I began to recall: "So a bachelor's thesis is like this!"

Of course, for his troubles, I also felt extremely sympathetic.

Complexion Problems

Female Assistant's Meal 220

Last year, a certain organization needed someone proficient in small regular script, so they posted a small advertisement seeking applicants. They received a total of three hundred applications, overwhelming the organization, which didn't know how to choose. A shop that collected the letters even had applicants coming to their door, willing to spend several foreign dollars for the shop's staff to have a feast. Hearing this, I knew how difficult it was for men to find work and how many were unemployed. I boldly assumed that women's employment would not be so dire.

Recently, I heard that a certain organization was recruiting a female assistant, and the result was the opposite of what I had imagined. The organization, imitating the regulations of the Young Women's Christian Association, planned to have a woman handle mail, which was essentially a disguised "messenger" position. It was said that the monthly salary was only ten dollars, and the applicants included middle school dropouts, kindergarten nannies, primary school teachers, hospital nurses, women in cheongsams and leather shoes, with powdered faces and short hair, mostly young women. The organization was astonished, feeling it unbearable to have them do this work, and without any better positions to place them. They never imagined that such a recruitment would result in such a tragic spectacle of female unemployment!

They even said repeatedly: "We don't care about the salary; we can endure hardship." Some even asked for an immediate resolution.

In the past, people said, "Wearing silk, eating oil in the belly." But are they not wearing silk? Now, it's clear that it's not necessarily the case; it's just putting on a brave face. The one finally chosen, it was said, had a family who used to run a shop in Zhabei. After the Shanghai Incident, the whole family was ruined, and she lost her job... But people continued to arrive despite the rain, and even after hearing that someone had been "selected," they still stubbornly said, "I'm just asking for a friend." How heartbreaking and shameless this is! I don't know if it's a gift from the violent sun, or if society has reached this point? Thinking about this, I'm also shocked by how many dancers, singers, and prostitutes there are.

Street Tail

Loyal and Upright, Bearing the Name of Zai Changwu 221

Walking past Zhengjia Wood Bridge, I saw many people standing in front of a hotel entrance, looking at the wall. Unconsciously, I squeezed in to join the crowd. The first thing I saw was a neatly written sign that read "Dr. of Literature ×× is a guest." Next to it, arranged on both sides, were several small photos. Who were the people in the photos? They were all important figures in the party and the nation. But there was also an exception: a photo of the "Manchurian Chief Executive," who had been kidnapped by the Japanese and made the protagonist of a puppet show in Manchukuo.

"This is another advertisement from a boring street performer," I thought, understandingly. At the same time, I wanted to leave, because such tricks were commonplace in Shanghai, nothing more than selling "wild man's head" to earn a living, praising and extolling successful figures, and making imperfect criticisms and accusations of past celebrities. But it was the first time I had encountered a street performer with a doctorate in literature. In order to glimpse the doctor's knowledge, I lingered to watch. Under each photo was a sentence that was neither poetry nor commentary. The last photo was of a young man in military uniform, labeled with the five characters "True Portrait of Zhang Xueliang." I thought, this

is a leader who became famous for allowing two provinces to be ceded without resistance in a short period, a fortune teller who is best at catering to trends. I wonder what kind of criticism he has? Looking closely, it was also four lines of poetry:

Round face, thick eyebrows, wide cheeks and chin,

High ears, fleshy, even black eyes,

Body like a unicorn, strong and majestic,

Loyal and upright, bearing a unique name.

The words "round face, fine eyebrows" didn't seem to describe the true appearance of the young master Zhang. I repeated the phrase "Loyal and upright, bearing a unique name," and couldn't help but laugh. What a flattering Dr. of Literature! It's a pity he lives in Shanghai. If he were around Zhang Xueliang, he would definitely be appreciated and perhaps recommended for an official position!

Leading hundreds of thousands of troops, he did not resist foreign insults, but indulged in pleasure and extravagance. Nothing could be worse. And this so-called Dr. of Literature uses him as a front and even praises him with the beautiful name of "loyal and upright." I don't know what to say?

What a loyal and upright Zhang Xueliang, now he has found a confidant, truly worthy of everlasting fame!

Civil First Instance Judgments: Zhang Zixin vs. Cheng Fuqing, loan case: Defendant Cheng Fuqing shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan, with annual interest of 2% from November 28, 1931, until the date of completion of the execution. If he cannot repay, Defendant Zhang Nan Yin shall be responsible for repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Cheng Fuqing. ▲ Amu Sheng vs. Sun Ahai, loan case: Defendant Xu Xinxun, i.e., Xu Xin, shall repay the plaintiff 100 yuan. If he cannot repay, Defendant Sun Ahai shall be responsible for repayment. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Xu Xinxun, i.e., Xu Xin. ▲ Yi Yu Hao Zhang Bingsheng vs. Wu Riyong, debt case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,100 yuan, with monthly interest of 1% from February 29, 1931, until the date of completion of the execution. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Xu Wenzhao vs. Wu Shusheng, loan case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 300 yuan, with annual interest of 2% from September 1, 1931, until the date of repayment. This amount shall be repaid at 50 yuan per month until fully repaid. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Shang Binghua vs. Yang Genlin, request for separation from family and delivery of a single inheritance: The plaintiff is granted separation from the family and shall live separately from the defendant. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Huang Shixi vs. Zhi He Yong Money Shop, bill case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,200 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Xie Tai Sheng vs. Shen Huikang, loan case: The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 790 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Mikladze vs. Xue Men Mikladze, divorce case: The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Civil Instructions: Cai Linqing vs. Yu Kangrong et al., debt case, request for cancellation of the case: The request for cancellation is approved; one copy of the settlement agreement is kept for verification. ▲ Yu Tai Seafod Shop vs. Zhuang Yu Long Shop, goods case, request for cancellation of the case: The request for cancellation is approved. ▲ Meng Lai Sheng vs. Gu Xing Nan, debt case, request for execution: It is reported that the debtor has paid 32 yuan. You are instructed to come to the court to collect the money at 9:00 AM on the 13th of this month. ▲ Xie Cheng Brick and Ash Shop vs. Xin Jin Sheng, bill case, request for execution: You are instructed to issue a summons for investigation and recovery. ▲ Song Rongchuan vs. Sun Liechang, deposit case, request for execution: You are instructed to issue a summons for investigation and recovery. ▲ Qia Kete Lamu vs. Dai Xiangen, debt case, request to release the defendant: The request is approved. ▲ Chen Pinmei vs. Zhou Guisong, mortgage case, request for delivery of judgment: This case involves a final judgment that the debtor's mortgaged land be handed over to the creditor for management. Whether the houses attached to the land should be relocated is not within the scope of execution. You should file a separate lawsuit to resolve this issue. ▲ Wu Shaolin vs. Gao Youpan et al., guarantee case, request for prior compensation: Chen Yunqing has not yet paid off the debt. The case will be reviewed after the debt is paid off. ▲ Lin Yiquan vs. Wang Shunlai, rental case, request for execution: The relocation portion of this case was entrusted to the Shanghai Local Court for assistance on September 1, 1931, and the party was notified to apply to that court. You should directly request the removal from that court. ▲ Guan Xiangfa vs. Hongkou Hotel, deposit case, request for execution: You are instructed to issue a summons for investigation and recovery. ▲ Yang Chun Ji vs. Gu Dagui et al., debt case, request to stop the auction and unseal the property: The request to stop the auction is approved because the case has been settled. You are instructed to order the clerk to unseal the property. ▲ Cai Minjiang vs. Zheng Zirong, rent case, request to collect the case money: You are instructed to come to the court at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month to collect the money. ▲ Sen Sheng Company Yu Bao San vs. Jin Feng Gang, land rental case, declaration of objection: You are instructed to come to the court at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month for interrogation. ▲ Zhang Zhou Peiwen vs. Zhang Xiaobo, divorce alimony case, request for cancellation of the case: The request for cancellation is approved. ▲ Ke Nei Mo Ka vs. Zheng Zhiyuan, loan case, request for execution: You are instructed to continue to issue summons for interrogation and recovery. ▲ Hai Er Si Bo vs. Dong Zilian et al., debt case, request to collect the case money: You are instructed to come to the court at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month to collect the money. ▲ Chen Li Shi vs. Gong Yuetan et al., loan case, request to limit the guarantor's payment: It has been guaranteed by the guarantor that the payment will be made within two weeks. If the deadline is exceeded, a summons will be issued for recovery. ▲ Kong Qingping vs. Shao Qilin, debt case, request for cancellation of the case: The request for cancellation is approved. ▲ Chen Tingduo et al., request for a certificate to manage the inheritance: You are instructed to submit a photograph of the title deed and provide a supplementary description of the location of the inheritance for verification. ▲ Accountant Wang Yusheng, request to file the appointment as liquidator of Chenguang Art Photography Studio: It is reported that whether Chenguang Art Photography Studio is organized in accordance with the provisions of the Company Law and whether it has been registered in accordance with the law have not been clarified. Therefore, it is difficult for this court to approve the filing of the accountant's appointment as liquidator of the studio.

Criminal Instructions: Chen Luo Shi's request for bail: The case is under trial, so the request for parental bail is unnecessary. ▲ Wang Chenshi's request for a trace of her missing adopted daughter: Although the police station has been reported to investigate, the search should still be expedited. There is no need to file the case. You are instructed to notify.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 224

Civil Instructions: Chen Boqi's request to collect the money. You are instructed to come to the court at 10:00 AM on the 13th of this month to collect the money. ▲ Lu Gaoyong's request for execution. You are instructed to wait for the case to be heard and investigated. ▲ Qian Fucheng's request for provisional execution by providing security. Since security has been provided in accordance with the judgment, the request for provisional execution should be approved. ▲ Hanam Sheng's request for execution. Because the case is not finalized, the request for execution should be postponed. ▲ Zhenda Customs Broker's request for filing of the charge of using Hu Zhongji's Bai Youguang paper five pieces to offset the porterage fee. Because there are obvious disputes in the claims of the applicant, the request for filing cannot be approved. ▲ Vladimir Barbaek's request for limiting the plaintiff's return of the disputed case. Because the civil execution case has statutory reasons, the execution cannot be stopped because of the payment of the security deposit. The money paid by the applicant at the time of seizure has already been issued by this court to the creditor for collection and completion of the case. Therefore, the request to limit the creditor's return and storage of the case is without legal basis and cannot be approved. ▲ Wang Zhixian's request to be exempted from paying another security deposit and to be released quickly. The request is disapproved. You are still instructed to change the search for a proper security to be reviewed and approved. ▲ Xu Yutian's request for the issuance of arrest warrants and collection of evidence. The case has already been approved by this court to stop execution because the defendant filed a third-instance appeal, and the entire file has been sent to the High Third Sub-Court for processing. The various sections requested should be postponed. ▲ Xinkang Company's request to unseal the property. The request is approved. You are instructed to order the clerk to unseal the property. ▲ Qianyi Silver Company's request for forcible sale and execution. You are instructed to wait for the case to be heard and investigated. (June 8)

Fang Quanfu's sentence is suspended for two years. ▲ Wang A Jin, selling opium, sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined two hundred yuan. ▲ Wang Xiaogui, intending to profit by providing premises for others to smoke opium, sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan. ▲ Chen Jinfa, smoking opium, sentenced to two months of imprisonment, suspended for two years. ▲ Jiang A Jin, providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Wu Laibao, Du Adi, Gong Shaojin, Zhang Yongqi, and Ding Gushi, smoking opium substitutes, each sentenced to one month of imprisonment. ▲ Wu Laibao, Gong Shaojin, and Ding Gushi's sentences are suspended for two years each. ▲ Wang Mei, intending to profit by gathering people for gambling, sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan. ▲ Gu Hongtao, assault, fined thirty yuan. He is acquitted of the remaining charges. ▲ Police Station vs. Gao Yuqing et al., theft case. Gao Yuqing and Gao Jumin (i.e., Xiao Xiuying) are found not guilty. Zhang Lianfang, Gao Yunsheng, and Lu Changgen, smoking opium substitutes, each sentenced to one month of imprisonment. Chen Dongcheng, Gu Dekang, Wang Jincai, Qiu Yongyu, Kang Changgen, and Dai Guisheng, smoking opium substitutes, each sentenced to one month of imprisonment.

Criminal Instructions: Xu Zhiming's request to postpone the payment of the fine. Because the fine of 500 yuan and the attached civil suit portion of 300 yuan should be paid on June 11 and July 11 respectively, and cannot be violated or delayed, the request to postpone the payment is disapproved. (June 9)

Shanghai Local Court 225

Criminal Judgments: Wu Naiyan, smoking opium, sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined two hundred yuan. Chen Bangxian, smoking opium, sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan. Wu Naiyan and Chen Bangxian are found not guilty of the robbery charge. Zhu Asan's case is dismissed. ▲ Gao Shiyuan, illegally depriving others of their freedom of movement, sentenced to five months of imprisonment. ▲ Wang Wenbin, intending to profit by providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Tang Rongsheng and Tang Linshi, jointly committing theft during a disaster, each sentenced to six months of imprisonment.

Civil Judgments: Chen Chengshi vs. Chen Zhanyuan, rent arrears dispute. The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 102 yuan in rent arrears and return the leased land. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhou Jinkui et al. vs. Ni Nianshu, appeal against mortgage dispute. The appeal is rejected. The appeal costs shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Chongde Company vs. Wo Yinwu, rent dispute. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 198 yuan in rent and immediately vacate the premises. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff for three-fifths of the settlement portion and one-fifth of the withdrawn portion, and the defendant shall bear the remaining one-fifth. ▲ Hu Fusheng vs. Ye Maoru, appeal against goods payment dispute. The original judgment is changed. The appellant shall repay the appellee 20 yuan in goods payment. The appellee's remaining claims in the first instance are rejected. The appellee shall bear nine-tenths of the litigation costs in the first and present instance, and the appellant shall bear the remaining one-tenth.
